@b{Der}

[237.lpp.]
@v{Der Hymnus vnd Lobgeſang zum Advent;}
@l{Veni Redemtor gentium.}
1.
VNVn nahtz tahß Paſẜaules Peſtitais / 
Tahß Jumprawas Bährns atſihtz / 
Par ko ſöw brienoyahß wiſẜa Paſẜaule / 
Deewam tada Peedſimbſchana pattiek.
2. Nhe no Wiera Aſẜini / neds no Meeſẜu / 
Bett ween no to ſwätu Gharru / 
Gir Deewa Wahrdtz tappis Czillwähx / 
Vnd ſeed weenas Ꞩeewas Auglis.
3. Tahß Jumprawas Meeſẜa apgrutenata tappa / 
Tomähr pallicka Ghodtz ſkieſts pagglabbohts / 
Atſpiedeya daſchadi dawani krahßni / 
Deews by ẜawà Ghodibà.
4. Wings ißghaya aran ẜawu Kambari / 
To ſkieſtu Koniņja dſiewohkle / 
Patteeß Deews vnd Czillwäcks / 
Ꞩawu Czeļļu tätzädams ſteids.
5. Wings ißtetzeya no Thäwu / 
Vnd greeſehs atkal py Thäwu / 
Brautze Elles dibbinà / 
Vnd atkal py Deewa krähßlu.
6. Katters tu eſẜi tam Tähwam lieds / 
Vßwarri ẜawahß Meeſẜahß / 
Ka taws muhſchiex Deewiex Spähx / 
Eekſchan mums te wayu Meeſẜu vsturr.
7. Tawa Ꞩille ſpied ſpohſcha vnd krahßna / 
Tay Nacktei gir jauns Ghaiſchums / 
Tumbẜibai nhe buhs nahkt eekſchan /
Ta Titziba palieek allaſch ſkaidra.
@b{8 Gohtz}

[238.lpp.]
8. Gohdtz gir Deewam tam Tähwam ẜatzietz / 
Gohdtz gir Deewam wiņja Dählam / 
Gohdtz gir Deewam tam ſwätam Gharram / 
Allaſchien vnd muſchige / Amen.

@v{Jm Thon: Vom Himmel hoch da}
@v{kom ich her /} @l{etc.}
1.
SLawähtz gir taß wiſẜewallditais Deews / 
Katters par mums apſchläloyees gir / 
Vnd ẜuhtiyis ẜawu wiſẜemiļaku Dählu / 
No ẜöw dſimbtu auxtakà Ghohdà.
2. Ka taß muhſẜo Peſtitays taptu / 
Mums peſtitu no to Gräko Naßtu / 
Vnd czaur ẜawu Schälaſtibu vnd Taißnibu / 
Eewäßtu muhſchigà Skaidribbà.
3. O leela Schälaſtiba vnd Lehniba / 
O dſiļļa Mileſtiba!
Deews darra tahdu darrbu / katam nhe weens Czillwähx / 
Neds Engelis par to ghanne patteikt warr.
4. Deews vsjämm muhſẜu Czillwäzigu czhiemi / 
Taß Radditaiß wiſẜo leeto / 
Wings nhe apſmey weenu nabbagu Ꞩeewu / 
Ka tas Czillwähx taptu wiņjahß Meeſẜahß.
5. Ta Tähwa Wahrdtz no muhſchibas / 
Tohp Meeſẜa wiſẜà Schkieſtiba / 
Taß Eeẜakums vnde taß Ghalls / 
Dohdahß par mums leelohß bähdohß.
6. Kaß gir taß Czillwäx / kaß gir wiņja Darrbs / 
Ka deews ẜawu Dählu par to dohd ?
Kammehß wayagham tai auxtakai Manntai / 
Ka ta muhſẜo dehļ tha darra ?
@b{7. Ock}

[239.lpp.]
7. Ock way teems Ļaudeems / kattri töw nitzina / 
To Schälaſtibu nheẜayäm / 
Nhe gribb klauſẜiet tha Dähla Balxnu / 
Vs to palleek Deewa Dußmiba.
8. O Czillwähx / ka tu to nhe proht
Tawam Koniņjam prettie eedt / 
Katters py töw nahk tick Lehnpratiex / 
Vnd töwis tick ẜirdige aisjämmahß.
9. Ey vsjem to ſchodeen ar Preeku / 
Ꞩataiſẜi tam to Czellu tawahß Ꞩirdtz / 
Ka taß warr nahkt tawa Prahtà / 
Vnd tu dabbu no ẜawu Schälsſtibu.
10. Padohd tam tawu Ꞩapraſſchanu / 
Schini ſchehlighà Attnahkſchanà / 
Padohd wiņja Swehtibai
Tohß darrbus tawas Taißnibas.
11. Ja tu to darri / tad buhß wings taws / 
Paſẜargha töw par tahß Elles Mohkas / 
Ja nhe / tad töw labb ẜarghayeeß / 
Aiſto wings töw aißlähds tahß Debbeſẜes Durrwis.
12. Ꞩawa pirrma Attnahkſchana ſchinni Paſẜaule / 
Gir bijuſẜi ļohte lehniga / 
Ta ohtra buhß ļohte barrga / 
Teems Beßdeewigeems par leelu Mohku.
13. Bett tee kattri eekſchan CHriſto ſtahw / 
Ee=eeß tad leelà Preezibà / 
Vnd buhß py to Engeļo Drauds / 
Ka teems nheneekada Nhelaime wairs kaitehß.
14. Tam Tähwam auxtà Ghodibà
Ar ẜawu weenu peedſimbtu Dählu / 
Ta lieds aridſan tam ſwätam Gharram
Gir Gohdtz vnd Slawa muhſchige / Amen.
@b{Magnifi-}

[240.lpp.]
@l{Magnificat.}
Manna Dwehẜele teitz to Kunghu / vnd mans Gharrs epreezeenayahß
par to Deewu mannu Peſtitayu.
Aiſto taß gir to Sämmoſchanu ẜawas Kallpones
vsraudſiyis / Redſi no ſcho laiku man ẜwatu teix wiſẜi Bährno
Bährni.
Aiſto taß gir leelu leethu py man darriyis / katters Spehziex gir/
vnd kattra wahrtz Ꞩwähtz gir.
Vnd wiņja Schälaſtiba palleek no weenas Czilltas ihs ohtras
/ py teems / kattri to biya.
Tas gir ſpehziex ar ẜawu Ällkonu / vnd ißkaiſẜa tohß kattri
gräſni gir ẜawas Ꞩirtz prahta.
Tas gruhſch tohß Spehzigus no to Krähſlu / vnd pazeļļ
tohs Ꞩämmoſchus auhſcham.
Tohs Jßallkuſchus peepillda tas arr Labbibu / vnd attſtay
tohs Bagaatus tuckſchus.
Tas peeminn tahß ſchälaſtibas / vnd vspallieds ẜawam Kallpam{Kallpani}
Jſrael.
Ka tas gir runnayis muhſẜeems Thäweems / Abraham vnd 
wiņja Ꞩäklam muhſchige.
Gohdtz gir tam Thäwam / tam Dählam / vnd tam ſwätam
Gharram / Ka no pirrmo Eeẜakumu gir biyis / vnd palleeck muhſchige
muhſcham / Amen.

II,
@v{Von der Geburt JEſu CHriſti.}
CHriſtum buhs mums ſlaweht krahßne / 
Tahs ſkieſtas Jumprawas Marias Dählu / 
Tick tahļ ka tha Myļa Ꞩaule ſpied /
Vnd ihs wiſſas Paſẜaules ghalla ſteepiahs.
2. Tas ſwähtz Radditays wiſẜas leetas
Apwilka Kalpa wayu Meeſẜu /
Ka tas to Meeſẜu czaur to Meeſẜu atpeſtitu / 
Vnd wiņja Raddiyums wißkim nhe taptu ẜamaitahtz.
3. Ta Deewa ſchälaſtiba no auxtu Debbeſẜu / 
Eeekſchan tahs ſkieſtas Mahtes Meeſẜas eedohdahs / 
Weena Meitiņja näß weenu ſläppänu Naßtu / 
Kattru ta Meeſẜa nhe paſinna.
4. Tas ghodiex Namms tahs krahßnas Ꞩirdtz / 
Peepehſch Deewa Baſniza tohp / 
Kattra nhe weenu Wyru aiſkare neds adſinna / 
No Deewa Wahrdu ta apgrutenata attraßta tappa.
5. Ta czeenigha Mahte gir to pedſimmuſſi / 
Kattru Gabriels papreekẜche peeẜatziya /
Kattru ſwähtz Janis ar Läkſchanu paradiya /
Kad tas wehl ẜawas Mathes Meeſẜahs ghulleya.
@b{6. Taß}

[245.lpp.]
6. Tas ghulleya Ꞩeenà ļohte nabbax /
To czeetu Ꞩilliet tas nhe apnicka / 
Maß Peens wiņja barriba by / 
Katters nhe weenu Puttniņju ißalckt licka.
7. Ta Debbeſẜa draudſiba tadehļ preezayahs /
Tee Engeļi dſeed Deewam Ghohdu / 
Teems nabbageems Ghanneems tohp ſluddenahtz / 
Tas Ghanns vnd Radditais wiſſas Paſẜaules. 
8. Slawa / Ghohdtz vnd Patteitziba gir thöw ẜatzieta / 
Chriſte / pedſimbtz no ſkieſtas Jumprawas / 
Ar Tähwu / vnd to ſwähtu Gharru / 
No ſcho laiku muhſchige / Amen.

@v{Gelobet ſeiſtu JEſu CHrist.}
SLawähtz eſẜi tu JEſu CHriſt / 
Ka tu Czillwähx peedſimmis eſẜi / 
No weenas Jumprawas / taß gir teeß /
Tapehtz preezayahß ta Engelo draudſe / Kyrie eleiẜon.
2. Tha muhſchiga Thäwa weeniex Bährns
Taggad eekſchan Ꞩilles tohp attraſts / 
Eekſchan muhſẜu nabbagu Meeſẜu vnd Aſẜini
Aptehrpyas tha muhſchiga Baggatiba / Kyrie leiẜon.
3. Kattru wiſẜa Pasaule nhe apthwerr / 
Tas ghull eekſchan Marias klähpi / 
Tas gir weens maß Behrnings tappis / 
Katters wiſẜas leetas weens vsturr / Kyrie eleiẜon.
4. Tas muhſchiex Ghaiſſchums eedt ſcheit eekſchan / 
Dohd tay Pasaulei jaunu ſpiedumu / 
Tas ſpied labb widdu paſẜchà nackty / 
Vnd mums parr Ghaiſſchumas Bährnus darra / Kyrie eleiẜon.
5. Tas Dähls ta Thäwà ihſtens Deews / 
Weens Weeſẜis Paſẜaule tappa / 
@b{Vnd}

[246.lpp.]
Vnd wedde mums no ſchahß Paſẜaules / 
Vnd darra mums parr Behrnus ẜawà Wallſtibà / Kyrie eleiſon.
6. Tas gir Wirſẜon Semmes nahtzis nabbahx /
Ka tas par mums apſchälotohs / 
Vnd Debbeſẜys darritu baggatus /
Vnd ẜaweems myļeems Engeļeems liedſa / Kyrie eleiſon.

Ꞩawu leelu Mylaſtibu ar to parradiet /

@l{Grates nunc omnes.}

LAideeta mums wiſẜeems patteickt / Deewam muhſẜam Kungham
/ katters czaur ẜawu ſwähtu Peedſimbſchanu mums gir
attpeſtiyis no tha Wällna Spähku vnd Wallſtibu.
Tam peedärrahß / ka mehs ar teems Engeļeems dſeedam / allaſchien
Ghohdtz gir Deewam eekſchan Auxtiba.

@v{Vom Himmel hoch da kom ich her.}

NO auxtu Debbeſẜu es atteemu / 
Es attnäſẜu jums labbu jaunu Wehſt / 
Tas labbahs Wehſtes es tick dauds attnäſẜu / 
No teems es dſeedaht vnd runnaht gribbu.
2. Jums gir ſchodeen weens Behrnings peedſimmis / 
No weenas ißrädſätas Jumprawas / 
Weens Behrnings tick ſkaiſts vnde Krahßnis / 
Tam buhs juhſẜo Preekam vnd jaukumam buht.
3. Tas gir tas Kunx Chriſtus muhſẜo Deews / 
Tas gribb jums weſt no wiſẜu ļaun / 
Tas gribb patz juſſo Peſtitais buht / 
No Wiſẜeems Ghräkeems darriet ſkieſtus.
@b{4. Taß} 

[247.lpp.]
4. Tas attnäß jums wiſſu ſchälaſtibu / 
Kattru Deews tas Täws gir ẜattayſẜiyis / 
Ka jums ar mums Debbeſẜies / 
Buhs dſiewot nu vnd muhſchige.
5. Tad jemmeeta währa to ihſtänu Siem / 
To Ꞩilli / vnd ſkrandainus Autiņjus / 
Tur attrodaht juhs to Behrniņju /
Katters wiſẜu Paſẜaul vsturr vnd näß.
6. Tapehtz laideeta mums wiſẜeems preezateeß / 
Vnd ar teems Ghanneems eet eekſchan /
Paluhkoht ko Deews mums gir ſkinkoyis / 
Ar ẜawu myļu Dählu apghadayis.
7. Jemm währa manna Ꞩirdtz / vnd paluko /
Kas ghull turr eekſchan Ꞩillites / 
Kam pedärr tas krahßnis Behrnings / 
Tas gir tas myļais JEſulins.
8. Ꞩummähtz atnahtz tu ghodiex Weeſẜis / 
To Grehzeneeku nhe eſẜi apſmadeyis / 
Vnd nahtz py man eekſchan Waidu / 
Ka buhs man töw par to patteikt.
9. O Kunx tu Radditayis wiſẜo leeto /
Ka eſẜi tu tappis tick ſemmiex/
Ka tu teh ghulli ẜawituſẜchà Ꞩeenà / 
No kattru Lohps vnd Eſelis ähd.
10. Vnd jebſch ta Paſẜaule buhtu daudskahrt tick platta / 
No dahrgheems Ackmineems vnd Saltu darrita / 
Tad buhtu ta töw tock dauds maſa /
Par weenu ſchauru Schupuliet.
11. Tas Blaweris / vnd tahs Sieſchadrehbes / 
Gir rupſch Ꞩeens vnd Lackatingi/
Vs ko tu Konings tick leels vnd baggahts
Läppo / iht buhtu tee tawa Däbbäſẜa Wallſtiba.
@b{12. Tas}

[248.lpp.]
12. Tas gir töw ta nu pattitzis / 
Ka tu man teeſcham{teeſchani} radietu / 
Ka wiſẜahs Paſẜaules Spähx / Ghohtz vnd Mannta / 
Prekſchan töw nhe maxa / nhe pallieds / neds darra.
13. Ock mans wiſẜomiļais JEſulins / 
Darrees ẜöw ſkieſtu miextu Ghulltinyu /
Paduſẜehtees eekſchan mannas Ꞩirdtz Wahzinyu / 
Ka es töwis muhſcham nhe aismirſtu.
14. No to es allaſch lyxmis äßmu / 
Lähkoht vnd dſeedaht allaſchien / 
To ihſtänu midſänamu dſeeßmu / 
Ar Ꞩirdtz Preeku iick krahßne.
15. Ghohdtz vnd Ꞩlawa gir Deewam eekſchan auxtu krähßlu / 
Kas mums eeſkinko ſawu weenigu Dählu / 
Par to preezayahs to Engelo draudſe / 
Vnd dſeed mums tahdu jaunu Ghaddu.

@v{Vom Himmel kam der Engel ſchar.}
NO Däbbäſẜu nahtze to Engeļo Draudſe / 
Paradiyahs teems Ghanneems ſkaidre /
Tee ẜatziya teems / Wens krahßnis Behrnings /
Tur ghull eekſchan czeetu Ꞩill.
2. Eekſchan Bettlehem Davida Pilli /
Ka Micha to gir ſluddenayis / 
Tas gir tas Kunx JEſus CHriſt / 
Katters juhſẜo wiſẜo Peſtitais gir.
3. Tapehtz buhs jums iht preezigeems buht / 
Ka Deews ar jums gir ẜaliedſenayees /
Tas gir peedſimmis juhſẜo Meeß vnd Aſẜins /
Juhſſo Brahlis gir ta muhſchiga Mannta.
4. Ko warr jums kaiteht Grähki vnd Nahwe / 
Ar jums gir tas patteeſẜe Deews /
@b{Laid}

[249.lpp.]
Laid duſſmo Wälls vnd ta Elle /
Deewa Dähls gir tappis juhſẜo Draux.
5. Tas nhe warr neds gribb jums atſthawet /
Metteeta vs to juſẜu czerribu /
Laid juhs ghanne dauds kahrdena /
Tam gir Kauns / kas to nhe warr czeeſt.

	2. Vnd vs raudſiyis mannu Sämmoſchanu / 
No ſcho laiku man wiſẜur /
Jck kattris teix ſwähtu / 
Tu eſẜi leelu Leetu py man darriyis.
	3. Tu eſẜi arridſan ſpehziex myļais Kunx / 
Taws leels ſpähx muhſchige nhe nomirrſt / 
Taws Wahrdtz gir ļohte czeenitins / 
Tapehtz töw ick kattris ſlahwe vnd ghoda.
	4. Tu apſchäloyeeß par wiſẜeems / 
Kas töw no Ꞩirdtz byſtahs / 
@b{Vnd}

[298.lpp.]
Vnd palliedſi teems Nabbageems allaſchien / 
Kad teems buhß leelus bähdus czeeſt.
	5. Tha Czillwäka Lappnibai buhß ißniekt / 
Prett tawu Rohku nhe warr nheneeka paſtaweht / 
Kas ẜöw paļauyahß vs ẜawu Leppnibu / 
Tam tu dries pa ghallam ſteids.
	6. Tu ißnitzini to Czillwäko Paddomu / 
Tee gir Kunx tawi brieniſki darrbi / 
Ko tee prettie töw dohma / 
Tas noteek allaſch attpackaļ.
	7. Kas ſemmiex gir vnde mas / 
Py to tu parradi tawu Deewiſku Spähku / 
Vnd liedſini to weenam Leelam Kungham / 
Tohß Baggatus darri nabbagus / tohß Nabbagus baggatus.
	8. To tu Kunx darri ſchinnieß laikohs / 
Vnd atghadayeeß tahs Schälaſtibas / 
Jſraëļem tu gribbi palliedſeht / 
Tas gir taws ißrädſähtz Pullx.
	9. Mehs nhe äſẜam to no töw nopellniyuſchi / 
Tu eſẜi mums ļohte ſchehliex / 
Muhſẜeems Tähweems gir runnahtz / 
Weens Wahrdtz to eſẜi tu attghadayeeß.
	10. Arridſan Abrahamam tam petitzigam Wieram / 
Tam eſẜi tu patz ſwehreyis / 
Vnd tam ẜohliyis to Däbbäſẜo Wallſtibu /
Vnd wiņja Ꞩähklai muhſchige.

XIII.
@v{Am Tage Micha?lis.}
@v{HERR GOtt dich loben alle wir. Jm Tohn:}
@v{CHriſt der du biſt der helle Tag.}
@b{Kunx}

[299.lpp.]
KVnx Deews wiſẜi mehs töw teitzam / 
Vnd buhs ka peedärr töw patteickt / 
Par to Raddibu to krahßno Engelo /  
Kattri apkahrt töw ſtahw tawà Wallſtibà. 
2. Tee ſpied ſpohſch vnd ļohte krahßne / 
Vnd räds töw jhten patteeß /  
Tawu Ballxni tee allaſchien dſirrd / 
Vnd gir pilli Deewiſkas Ghuddribas.
3. Tee nhe duſẜahs no darrbu / ney ghull / 
Tee ween vs to ghahda /  
Ka tee Kunx Chriſt apkahrt töw gir /  
Vnd apkahrt tawu nabbagu Pullzinyu.
4. Ta wätza Tſchuhßka taß ļauns Waideneex /
No Eenaidu vnd Dußmibas dägg / 
Wings ween vs to dohma /  
Ka tas tawu Pullku trambditu.
5. Vnd ka tas pirmahk to Paſẜaul / 
Gir Nhelaimibà weddis / tha tas wehl darr / 
Baſnizus / Deewa Wahrdu vnd Ghohdu / 
Tas allaſchien gribb delldeht.
6. Tapehtz tas muhſcham nhe duß / 
Ruhtz ka kahtz Lawis / dohma allaſchien /  
Leek Spohſtus / Wallgus vnd Tihklus / 
Ka tas ẜamaitatu kas Deewam pa prahtam gir.
7. Teekams gir mohdriga to Engeļo Pullx / 
Kattri CHriſto allaſch pehtz ſtaiga / 
Vnd ghelb to Chriſtitu Draudſibu /  
Stahwädami prett tha Wälla Willtibu.
8. Py Danielu mhes to rädſam /  
Ka tas ſtarpan teems Laweems ẜehdeya /  
Ta Lieds arridſan to rahmu Loth /  
Tas Engels palliedſeya to no wiſẜu Nhelaimibu.
@b{9. Ta}

[300.lpp.]
9. Ta lieds arridſan tahs Vgguns Lähßmi / 
Nheneekad nhe warreya kaiteht /  
Teems Puyſſcheems tahdà Karrſtumà / 
Tas Engels teems palliedſeya. 
10. Tha ghlabbo Deews wehl taggadien / 
Par Nheilaim vnd daſchu Ꞩährgu /  
Mums czaur teems myļeems Engeliſcheems /  
Kattri mums par Ꞩarrgeems dohti gir .
11 . Tapehtz mehs töw ka peedärr ſlahweyam /  
Vnd patteitzam töw Deews muhſchige /  
Ka arridſan to myļo Engeļo Draudſe /  
Töw teitz ſchodeen vnd muhſchige.
12 . Vnd luhdſam töw / tu gribbähtu pawehleht /  
Ka tee allaſchien ghattawi gir. 
Ghlabboht tawu maſu Pullzinyu /  
Katters tawu Deewiſku Wahrdu czeeni.

@v{Collect auff Michaëlis.}
KVnx Deews däbbäſẜu Thäws / katters tu tawus 
Engeļus teems Czillwäkeems peelitzis eſẜi / tohs 
prettibe tha Wälla Willtibu vnd tahs Paſẜaules 
Blehdibu paſẜarrgaht: Mehs luhdſam töw / tu ghribbätu
tahdu Ghlabboſchanu ſchehlige py mums vsturreth
/ vnd czaur tawu ſwähtu Gharru palliedſeht / ka
taws Prahtz py mums Czillwäkeems wirſẜo Semmes /
ka eekſchan Debbes no taweems Engeļeems noteek / ka 
mehs ſcheitan pehtz tawu Prahtu dſiewoyam / vnd turr 
muhſchige töw ſlahweht warram; Czaur JEſum Chriſtum
tawu Dählu muhſẜu Kunghu: Amen. 
@b{XIV. Fol-}

[301.lpp.]
XIV.
@v{Folgen Geſänge von den Zehen Geboten.}
@v{Diß ſind die helgen Zehn Gebot.}
SChee gir tee ſwäti deßmitti Baußli /  
Kattrus mums dewe Deews muhſẜo Kunx /  
Czaur Moſen ẜawu myļu Kallpu / 
Vs Sinai paſſchà Kallnà ghallà / Kyrie eleiſon.
2. Es weens äßmu taws Deews vnd Kunx /  
Nhe weenus Deewus buhs töw wairs czeeniet /  
Vs man buhs töw wißkim paļautees /  
No Ꞩirdz dibben man myļoht / Kyrie eleiſon.
3. Töw nhe buhs nhepatteeß wallkoht /  
Deewa tawa Kungha Wahrdu / 
Töw nhe buhs teickt pareiſe neds labb / 
Beß to ko Deews patz ẜacka vnd darra / Kyrie eleiſon.
4. Töw buhs ſwehtiet to ẜeptitu Deenu /  
Ka tu vnd taws Namms duſẜeht warr /  
Töw buhß atſtaht no tawu Darrbu / 
Ka Deews ẜawu Darrbu eekſchan töw darryth warr / Kyrie eleiſon.
5. Töw buhß ghohdaht vnd paklauſẜigam buht /  
Tawam Tähwam vnd tawai Mahtei / 
Vnd kur tawa Rohka teems palliedſeht warr /  
Tad tu illge dſiewoſẜi / Kyrie eleiſon.
6. Töw nhe buhß dußmoth / neds nokaut /  
Ney eeniedeht / neds patts attreeptees / 
Bett czeeſt vnd lähnu Prahtu turreht / 
Vnd arridſan tawam Eenaidneekam labb darryth / Kyrie eleiſon.
7. Tawu Laulibu buhs töw ſkieſte paſẜargaht / 
Tha ka tawa Ꞩirdtz vs czittu wairs nhe czerre / 
@b{Vnd}

[302.lpp.]
Vnd turreht ſkieſt tawu Dſiewibu / 
Ar Ghohdu vnd ghaddibu krahßne / Kyrie eleiſon.
8. Töw nhe buhß Naudu neds Manntu ſackt /  
Neds nhepatteeß jembt otru ſweedru vnd Aſẜini /  
Töw buhß atdarrieth tawu ſchehligu Rohku / 
Vnd teems Nabbageems darryht labbe / Kyrie eleiſon.
9. Töw nhe buhß nhepatteeſẜu Leezibu doht /  
Neds mäloht vs tawu Tuwaku / 
Wiņja Nhenoſeedſibu buhß töw aißbildeht /  
Vnd wiņja Kaunu aißklaht / Kyrie eleiſon.
10. Töw nhe buhß tawa Tuwaka Ꞩeewu vnd Nammu /  
Vnd wiß kas tam peedärr / nhe eekahrohtees / 
Töw buhs tam wehleht wiſẜu labb /  
Ka töw tawa Ꞩirdtz paſſcham darra / Kyrie eleiſon. 
11. Tee Baußli wiſẜi mums dohti gir / 
Ka töw tawus Ghräkus / o Czillwäka Bährs /  
Atſieth buhß / vnde mahzieth labb / 
Ka töw preekſchan Deewu dſiewoht buhß / Kyrie eleiſon. 
12. To palliedſa mums muſẜo Kunx JEſus CHriſt /  
Katters muhſẜo Widdetaiß tappis gir /  
Wiß muhſẜo Darrbs gir paſuſts /  
Mehs wairs nhe pällnam ka Deewa Dußmibu / Kyrie eleiſon.

@b{Menſch wiltu leben ſeliglich.}
CZillwähx gribbi tu dſiewoht ſwehtige /  
Vnd py Deewu pallickt muhſchige /  
Tad buhß töw turreht tohß deßmittes Baußlus /  
Kattrus mums muhſẜo Deews pawehļ / Kyrie eleiſon.
2. Es weens äßmu taws Deews vnd Kunx /  
Töw nhe buhß czittu Deewu czeenieth / 
Tawai Ꞩirrdei buhß ẜöw vs man paļauteeß /  
Manna paſſcha Wallſtiba buhß töw buht / Kyrie eleiſon.
@b{3. Töw}

[303.lpp.]
3. Töw buhß mannu Wahrdu ghodaht krahßne /  
Vnd tawohß bähdohß mann peeẜaukt / 
Töw buhß ſwehtiet to ẜwähtu Deenu / 
Ka Eß eekſchan töw ſtrahdaht warru / Kyrieleyſon.
4. Tam Tähwam vnde tay Mahtey /  
Buhß töw ka man paklauſẜiet /  
Nehweenu nokaut / neds dußmigam buht /  
Vnd tawu Laulibu turreht ſkieſte / Kyrieleiſon.
5. Töw nhe buhß arridſan nheneek Sackt /  
Vs nheweenu nhepatteeſẜu Leezibu doht /  
Tawa Tuwaka Ꞩeewu nhe eekaroth / 
Vnd no wiſẜu wiņja Paddomu labpraht attſtahteeß / Kyrie eleiſon.

XV.
@v{Vom H. Chriſtlichen Glauben.}
@v{Wir gläuben all an einen GOtt.}
MEhß titzam wiẜi eekſchan weenu Deewu / 
Radditayam Debbeß vnd tahß Semmes /  
Kas ẜöw par Tähwu dehweeß gir /  
Ka mehs wiņja Bährni tohpam: 
Tas ghribb mums allaſch barryoht /  
Meeſẜu vnd Dwehſẜeli arridſan labbe ẜarrgaht /  
Wiſẜu ļaunu ghribb tas no mums noghreeſt /  
Nheneeka ļaun buhß mums notickt /  
Tas ghada par mums /  
Ghlabboſchana vnd Ꞩarrghaſchana /  
Tas ſtahw wiß eekſchan wiņja Spehku. 
2. Mehß titzam arridſan eekſchan JEſum CHriſtum /  
Wiņja Dählam muhſẜam Kungham /  
Katters muhſchige py to Tähwu gir / 
@b{Lieds}

[304.lpp.]
Lieds weens Deews no Spähku vnd Ghohdu / 
No Marias tahs ſkieſtahs Jumprawas /  
Gir weens pattees Czillwähx peedſimmis / 
Czaur to ſwähtu Gharru eekſchan Titzibas / 
Par mums / kattri mehs biyam paſudduſſchi / 
Py Kruſtu nomirriß / 
Vnd no to Nahwu / 
Attkall aukſcham czehleeß czaur Deewu.
3. Mehß titzam arridſan eekſchan Swähtu Gharru / 
Deews ar to Tähwu vnd to Dählu /  
Katters wiſẜo behdigo Eepreezeetaiß gir / 
Vnd ar Dahwaneems aptährp krahßne /  
Tohs wiſẜus Chriſtitus wirſẜon Semmes /  
Turr eekſchan weenu Prahtu liedſiege /  
Scheit wiſẜi Ghräki pammäſti tohp /  
Tai Meeſẜi buhß arridſan atkall dſiewoht /  
Pehtz ſchahß behdigas dſiewoſchanas /  
Gir ghattawa darritha / 
Mums weena dſiewoſchana muhſcham beß ghallu.

@v{Jch gläub an GOtt.}
ES titzu Deewam Tähwam / Wiſẜewallditayam /
Radditayam Debbeß vnd tahs Semmes. Vnde
JEſum CHriſtum wiņja weeniga Dählam / muhſẜam
Kungham : Katters eejämbtz gir no to ſwähtu
Gharru / peedſimmis no Marias tahs Jumprawas:
Mohzietz gir appakſchan Pontio Pilato / Kruſta ẜiſtz / nomirris
/ vnde appracktz / ſemme kahpis eekſchan Elles /  
Treſſchà deenà atkal aukſcham czehleeß no tas Nahweß :
Vsbrautzis Debbeſẜihß / Ꞩeedeeß py labbahs Rohkas 
@b{Deewa}

[305.lpp.]
Deewa ta Wiſẜewallditaya Tähwa : No turrenes tas
attkall nahx ẜohdiet tohß dſiewus vnd Nomirruſchus.
Eß titzu ſwähtam Gharram / Weenu ſwähtu Chriſtitu
Baſnizu / weenu Draudſibu to Swähto / Pammeſſchanu
to Ghräko / Aukſcham czellſchanu tohß 
Meeſẜas / vnd weenu muhſchigu dſiewoſchanu / Amen.


XVI.
@v{Vom Heiligen Vater Vnſer.}
MVhſẜo Tähws eekſchan Däbbäſẜo Wallſtibas / 
Katters tu mums wiſẜeems lieds pawehl /  
Brahļeems buht / vnd töw peeẜauckt / 
Vnd gribbi to Luhkſchanu no mums / 
Dohd ka nhe ween luhds ta Mutte / 
Palliedſi ka ta eeth no Ꞩirdtz dibben. 
2. Swehtietz tohp taws czeeniex Wahrdtz / 
Palliedſi tawu Wahrdu py mums ſkieſt turreht / 
Ka mehs arridẜan ẜwehtige dſiewoyam / 
Pehtz tawu Wahrdu czeenige / 
Paſẜargi mums Kunx par willtigu Mahzibu / 
Tohß nabbagus peewilltus Ļaudis atgrees. 
3. Laid nahk tawa Wallſtiba ſchinny laikà / 
Vnd pehtz ſcho laiku muhſchige / 
Tas ſwähtz Gharrs mums dſiewo klaht / 
Ar ſaweems daſchadeems Dawaneems / 
Ta Wällà Dußmibu vnd leelu Warru / 
Ꞩalaus / preekſchan to tawu Baſnizu vsturri. 
4. Taws Prahtz laid no teek / Kunx Deews / ween lieds / 
@b{Wirß}

[306.lpp.] 
Wirß Semmes / ka Däbbäſẜa Wallſtibà /  
Dohd mums czeeſchanu behdigà laikà / 
Paklauſẜigeems buht labbà vnd ļaunà deenà /  
Stahw prettieb wiſẜu Meeſẜu vnd Aſẜini / 
Katters prett tawu Prahtu darra. 
5. Dohd mums ſchodeen muhſẜo deeniſku Maiß /
Vnd kaß Wayaga gir py Meeſẜas Vsturreſchanas / 
Paſẜargi mums Kunx par Eenaidu vnd Karryu / 
Par Nheweſẜelibu / vnd par dargu Laiku /  
Ka mehs labbà Meerà ſtahwam /  
To Ghahdibu vnd Nhegauſẜibu no mums ẜittam.
6. Wiſẜu muhſẜu Parradu peedohd mums Kunx /  
Ka tee mums wairahk Bähdus nhe darra / 
Ka mehs arridſan muhſẜeems Parradneekeems /  
Wiņjo Parradu labpraht peedohdam /  
Darri mums ghattawus wiſẜeems kallpoht /  
Eekſchan ihſtänu Myläſtibu vnd Weenaidibu.
7. Nhe wedd mums Kunx eekſchan Kahrdenaẜchanas /  
Kad mums tas ļauns Gharrs Kahrdina / 
Pa kreiſẜu vnd pa labbu Rohku /  
Palliedſi mums ſtippre prettieb ſtahweht / 
Eekſchan ſtippras Titzibas ẜattaiſẜiti / 
Czaur tawa ſwähta Gharra eepreezenaſchanu.
	8. No wiſẜu ļaun mums attpeſti / 
Nu gir tee laiki vnd deenas nickni /  
Peſti mums no to muhſchigu Nahwu /  
Vnd eepreezini mums paſtarà ſtundà /  
Dohd mums Kunx weenu ſchehligu Noſkirſſchanu / 
Jemm muhſẜu Dwehſẜel tawà Rohkà. 
9. Amen / tas gir / tas noteek pattees / 
Eeſtipprini muhſẜu Titzibu allaſchien / 
Ka mehs jo nhe alloyam py to / 
@b{Ko}

[307.lpp.]
Ko mehs ar ſcho Luhkſchanu luhguſchi äſẜam /  
Vs tawu Wahrdu eekſchan to Wahrdu JEſu /  
Ta ẜackam mehs no Ꞩirdtz / Amen.

@v{Ach Vater vnſer der du biſt im Himmelreich.}
OCh muhſẜo Tähws kas tu eſẜi eekſchan Däbbäſẜo Wallſtibas
/ auxte par mums / tapehtz Gharrà ghribbi no mums 
peeluhkts taptz / Taws ſwähtais Wahrdtz tohp ißplattietz ar 
leelu ſpähku / ghodahtz no mums vnde wiſẜur / eekſchan Debbes vnd
wirſẜon Semmes / Tahß ſchälaſtibas Wallſtiba nahk py mums / 
vnd laid py mums pallickt / vnd kas töw nhepatiek no mums / to 
ghribbätu tu ißdſiet / ka mehs warram muhſchige Tawà Wallſtibà
pallickt.
2. O ſwähtais Kunx mehs luhdſam töw / Taws Prahtz noteek /  
Wirſẜon Semmes ſcheit ka peedärr / Ka Däbbäſẜo Wallſtibà / Kur 
nhe weens nhe warr nahkt / neds paſtaweth / ka ween kas ſawu Prahtu
/ ar tawu ẜaliedſina: Vnd dohd mums muhſẜu deeniſku Maiß /  
Tay Meeſẜi ẜawu Barribu / Ta lieds Meeru ſchinny Semme / Nhekahda
Nheweſẜeliba parahdahß / Weenu ghodigu ghuddru Wirſẜeneeku
/ dohd Kunx töw par Ghohdu.
3. Muhſẜus Ghräkus vnd Noſegumus / mums arridſan Kunx 
peedohd / Ar kattreems mehs töw apkaitenayuſchi äſẜam / To mums 
nhe peelaghady : Aiſto mehs muhſẜeems Parradneekeems darram 
tha arridſan / Ar kattru tee mums apkaitenayuſchi gir / to ghribbam 
mehs wißkim aißmirrſt. Eekſchan Kahrdenaſchanas mums nhe 
eewedd / eekſchan kattras mehs warrätam ẜamaitaht / Par wiſẜu 
Ļaun mums paſẜargi / No kattru ta Dwehſẜele no mirrtu / vnd darri 
mums wiſẜus ween lieds par Bährneems tawà Wallſtiba.

@v{Ach Vater vnſer all. Jm Thon: Auff meinen}
@v{lieben GOTT.}
@b{Och}

[308.lpp.]
OCh muſẜo wiſẜo Tähws / katters tu Däbbäſẜo=wallſtiba
dſiewo Vnd pawehl mums nahkt / vnd no Ꞩirdtz töw peeẜaukt
/ Vs tahdu tawu ẜohliſchanu nahkam mehs vnd peeluhdſam
töw. 
2. Swehtietz tohp taws Wahrdtz / Tawa Wallſtiba py mums
nahk / Paſẜargi par willtigu Mahzibu / ta Wälla Wallſtibu ißpohſty
/ Taws Prahtz ta lieds vs Semmes noteek ka Däbbäſẜo=
wallſtibà. 
3. Dohd mums O myļais Deews / aran ſchälaſtibas to deeniſku 
Maiß / Vnd attpeſty mums arridſan no muhſẜeems ghruteems 
Ghräkeems / Tad ghribbam mehs arridſan labpraht peedohdt 
muhſẜeems Waideneekeems.
4. Tam Wällam prettie ſtahw / ka tas mums nhe peewiļļ /  
Nhe kahdà Kahrdenaſchanà eewädd / Neds py Jſẜamiſẜaſchanas 
ſpeeſch / Bett mums no wiſẜu ļaun / ſchehlige attpeßty.
5. Och myļais ſchehliex Kunx / ghauſẜini vnd wayro Mums
ſchahdu tawu Dawanu / kattru mehs dabbuyuſchi äſẜam / No tawas
leelas Lehnibas / Eſẜi mums ſchehliex allaſchien.
6. Aiſto O myļais Kunx / Töw peedärr Ghohdtz vnd Teickſchana
/ Tawa gir ta Wallſtiba / ta lieds arridſan ta Ghohdiba / Slawähtz
gir taws Wahrdtz / muhſchige muhſcham / Amen.

XVII.
@v{Von der heiligen Tauffe.}
@v{Chriſt vnſer HERR zum Jordan kam.}
CHriſtus muhſẜo Kunx py Jordanes nahze / 
Pehtz ẜawa Tähwa Prahtu : / : 
No to ſwähtu Jahni to Chriſtibu jehme /  
Ꞩawu Darrbu vnd Ammatu peepilldiet: 
@b{Tur}

[309.lpp.]
Tur gribbeya tas eeſtahdiet mums weenu Maßghaſchanu / 
Vnd maßghaht mums no Ghräkeems /  
Apſlietzenaht arridſan to ruhktu Nahwu /  
Czaur ẜawu paſſchu Aſſini vnd Mohkahms / 
Tas darriya mums weenu jaunu dſiewoſchanu.
2. Tad klauſẜeeta vnd jemmeeta wiſẜi währa /  
Ka Deews patz dehwe to Chriſtibu :/:
Vnd ko ick kattram Chriſtitam titzeht buhs / 
Ka tas warr atſtaht no willtigas Mahzibas /  
Deews ẜacka / vnd ghribb buhß Vhdenim buht /  
Bett nhe ween tyers Vhdens /  
Wiņja ſwähtz Wahrdtz gir arridſan klaht /  
Ar baggatu Gharru beß Mähru / 
Tas gir ſcheit patz tas Chriſtitais.
3. To gir tas mums ſkaidre parradiyis / 
Ar Siemehms vnd ar Wahrdeems :/:
Ta Tähwa Ballxnis tappa ſkannige / 
Turr patt py Jordanes dſirrdähtz /  
Wings ẜatziya / tas gir manns myļais Dähls / 
Py kataru man labs prahtz gir /  
To ghribbu es jums pawehleht / 
Ka jumms buhß to pareiſe klauſẜiet / 
Vnd darriet pehtz wiņja Mahzibu. 
4. Deewa Dähls arridſan patz ſcheit ſtahw / 
Eeekjchan ẜawu krahßnu Czillwäzibu :/:
Tas ſwahtz Gharrs no Däbbäſẜu nahk /  
Ar Balloſcha Czhimy apgherbees / 
Ka mums jo ſtippre titzeht buhs / 
Kad mehs Chriſtiti tohpam / 
Wiſẜa Triaidiba mums Chriſtiyuſſi gir /  
Ar to py mums wirſẜon Semmes /  
Dſiewoht gir ẜadderreyuſẜees.
@b{Saweems}

[310.lpp.]
5. Ꞩaweems Mahzekļeems pawehleya JEẜus CHriſt / 
Eidta wiſẜa Paſẜauleh mahziet :/: 
Ka ta eekſchan Ghräkeems paſuſta gir / 
Vnd buhs no Ghräkeems atſtahtees /  
Kas titz / vnd leekahß Chriſtitees /  
Tam buhs czaur to ſwähtam tapt / 
Weens jauns Czillwahx tas dähwähtz tohp / 
Katters muhſchige nhe warr mirrth / 
Tam buhß to Däbbäſẜu wallſtibu dabbuiht. 
6. Kaß nhe titz tahdai leelai ſchälaſtibai / 
Tas palleek ẜawohß Ghräkohs :/:
Vnd gir paſuddenahtz tai muhſchigai Nahwei / 
Dſiļļe Elles dibbinà / 
Tam nhe pallieds nheneek ẜawa Swehtiba /  
Wiß wiņja Darrbs gir paſuddis /  
Tee eedſimbti Ghräki to ẜamaita /  
Eekſchan kattreems tas gir peedſimmis / 
Neds ſpäh tam arridſan palliedſeht.
7. Ta Atz ween to Vdeni räds / 
Ka Czillwäki Vdeni ley :/: 
Ta Titziba eekſchan Gharru to ſpähku ẜaproht /  
No JEſu CHriſti Aſẜini / 
Vnd gir preekſchan to weena ẜarrkana Straume /  
No CHriſti Aſẜini ẜarrkana darrita /  
Kattra wiſẜu Wainu dſedina /  
Ko mehs no Adamu äſẜam dabbuyuſchi /  
Vnd arridſan paſſchi darriyuſchi.

XVIII.
@v{Von der Chriſtlichen Buſſe.}
@v{Auß tieffer Noht ſchrey ich zu dir.}
@b{Aran}

[311.lpp.]
ARan dſilleems bähdeems eß peeẜautẜu töw /  
Kunx Deews paklauſẜi mannu Ꞩaukſchanu :/:
Tawas ſchäligas Auſẜis grees py man / 
Vnd vs mannu Luhkſchanu tahs attwerr /  
Aiſto ja tu ghribbi to vsredſeht /  
Kas Ghräki vnd nhe patteeß gir darrietz / 
Kas warr / Kunx / tad preekſchan töw pallickt ?
2. Py töw nhemaxa nheneek ka ſchälaſtiba ween / 
Kad tu tohß Ghräkus peedohd :/: 
Tas gir tock wellte ar muhſẜu darrbu / 
Kad mehs wiß labbahke ghribbam dſiewoht / 
Preekſchan töw nhe warr nhe weens leelohtees /  
Tapehtz buhs ick kattram preekſchan töw bytees /  
Vnd tawu ſchälaſtibu ghaidiet.
3. Tapehtz ghribbu es vs Deewu czerreht / 
Vs mannu Nopällnu nhe luhkoht :/: 
Vs to mannai Ꞩirrdei buhß paļautees / 
Vnd vs wiņja Lehnibu titzeht /  
Kattru man ẜohla wiņja dahrx Wahrdtz / 
Tas gir mans Preex / vnd ſtippris Pills /  
To ghribbu es allaſchien ghaidiet. 
4. Vnd jeb tas kaweyahs ihß paſſchu Nackti / 
Vnd atkal ihß tam Rytam :/: 
Tomähr buhß mannai Ꞩirdei no Deewa Spähku / 
Nhe iſẜamiſt neds bähdatees /  
Tha darra Jſra?l ihſtäns Radtz /  
Katters no to Gharru raddietz gir / 
Vnd ẜawu Deewu paghaid. 
5. Jeb py mums gir dauds Ghräki / 
Py Deewu gir wairahk ſchälaſtibas :/: 
Wiņja Rohka nhe mitt pallidſeht / 
Czeek leela arridſan gir ta Waina / 
@b{Wings}

[312.lpp.]
Wings gir weens tas labbs Ghanns / 
Kas Jſra?l ißpeſtiet gribb / 
No wiſẜeems ẜaweems Ghräkeems.

@v{Erbarm dich mein O HErre GOtt.}
ABſchäloyees par man O Kunx Deews /  
Pehtz tawas leelas ſchälaſtibas : / : 
Nomaſga / darri ſkieſtus mannus Noſegumus / 
Eß atſiſtu mannus Ghräkus / tee man ruhp /  
Töw ween äßmu es ghräkoyis / 
Tas gir prettieb mann allaſchien /  
Tas ļauns preekſchan töw nhe warr paſtahweht / 
Tu palleetz taißnis / jeb tu ẜohdietz tohpi.
2. Raugi Kunx eekſchan Ghräkeems äßmu eß peedſimmis /  
Eekſchan Ghräkeems manna Mahte mann ẜayehme :/:
To Taißnibu tu myļo / vnd darri ſinnamu /  
Tawas ghuddribas apſlähptu Paddomu / 
Apſlatzini mann Kunx ar Jſopo / 
Es tohpu ſkieſts / ja tu maſga man / 
Balltahx nhe Sneex / Mannas Auſẜis tohp lyxmas / 
Wiſẜi manni Kauli eepreezenayahs. 
3. Kunx nhe vsluhko mannus Ghräkus / 
Leetz nohſt no mann wiſẜu Nhetaißnibu :/: 
Vnd darri ſkieſt eekſchan mann to Ꞩirrdi / 
Weenu jaunu Gharru eekſchan mann ghattawu darri /  
Nhe mett mann nohſt no tawu Waigu /  
Tawu ſwähtu Gharru nhe jemm no mann /  
To Preeku tawas Peſtiſchanas py mann attghrees /  
Tas paprahtiex Gharrs mann py töw vſturr. 
4. Teems Beßdeewigeems ghribbu es tawu Czeļļu / 
Teems Ghräzeneekems arridſan pamahziet :/: 
Ka tee no ļaunu willtigu czeļļu / 
@b{Czaur}

[313.lpp.]
Czaur töw py töw attgreeſchahs / 
Paſẜarrgi mann Kunx / Deews mannas Peſtiſchannas / 
Par to Ꞩohdu czaur Aſẜini eeſiemohtu /  
Manna Mehle paſluddena tawu yhſtänu Baußli /  
Dohd ka manna Mutte tawu Slawu ißplatta. 
5. Nhe weenu meeſẜigu Vpperi tu no mann praſẜi / 
Es buhtu töw to arridſan dewis :/: 
Tad jemm nu to ẜagrauſietu gharru / 
Weenu behdigu vnd noſkummuſku Ꞩirrdi turr klaht / 
Nhe ſmahde Deews to Vpperi /  
Darri labb pehtz tawas Lehnibas /  
Tam Kallnam Zion / kur Chriſtiti Ļaudis gir /  
Tee vppereh töw Tayßnibu.

@v{Derſelbige LI. Pſalm / auff eine andere}
@v{weiſe.}
@v{O HErre GOtt begnade mich.}
O Kunx Deews abſchäloyeeß par mann /  
Pehtz tawas lehnibas eſẜi man ſchehliex /  
Dellde mannu Noſegummu /  
Pehtz tawas leelas ſchälaſtibas :/: 
Vnd maſga mann ſkieſtu / O Kunx Deews /  
No wiſẜu mannu Noſegummu /  
Vnd darri mann ſkieſtu no Ghräkeems /  
Kattrus es eekſchan man attrohdu : 
Vnd manni Ghräki gir allaſch preekſchan mann /  
Es töw ween äßmu Ghräkoyis /  
Preekſchan töw äßmu es ļaun darriyis /  
Eekſchan taweems Wahrdeems tu paſtahweſẜi /  
Jeb tee tohp ẜohdieti. 
2. Raug eekſchan Nheghanntibu äßmu eß darrietz / 
@b{Ka}

[314.lpp.]
	Ka mann manna Mahte gir atnäſẜuſẜi / 
	Eekſchan Ghräkeems mann ẜayämuſẜi / 
	Dauds Ghräkus äßmu es darriyis :/: 
Bett ta Teeſẜiba töw pattiek / 
	Vnd dehwi mann arridſan ſinnaht / 
	Tawu ghuddribu beß bähdam / 
	Kattra gir apſlähpta:
Apſlacki mann ar Jſopo krahßne / 
Ka es tohpu ſkieſts / vnd maſga mann nu / 
Tick balltu ka Sneegu vnd Preeku leetz mann dſirrdeht / 
Ka te Kauli tohp lyxmi / 
Kattrus tu eſẜi ẜaſẜittis.
3. Nhe reds vs mannu ghrezigu dſimbtibu / 
	Dellde wiſẜus mannus Noſegumus / 
	Kunx tu ghribbätu eekſchan mann raddiet / 
	Weenu ſkieſtu Ꞩirrdi / vs to es czerru :/: 
Weenu patteeſẜu Gharru darri jaunu eekſchan man / 
	Nhe met mann arridſan wiſſkim no töw / 
	Nhe jemm no mann tawu ſwähtu Gharru / 
	Laid tas ar ẜawu ſchälaſtibu klaht ſtahw :
Vnd leetz man attkall attnahkt / 
To Preeku tawas Peſtiſchanas / O Deews mans Kunx / 
Tas drohſch Gharrs laid vsturr man / 
Tohs Beßdeewigus ghribbu es mahziet / 
Ka teems buhß ẜawu czeļļu vs töw greeſt.
4. No aſẜinaina Ghräkeems arridſan mann peſty / 
	O Deews tu mannas Peſtiſchanas Deews / 
	Ka manna Mehle warr paſluddenaht / 
	Tawu Taißnibu wiſẜaſke :/: 
Kunx attdarri mannas Luhpas / 
	Manna Mutte paſluddena tawu Ghohdu / 
	Töw nhe patiek tas Vpperis / 
@b{Es}

[315.lpp.]
Eß dohtu töw to arridſan / 
Dädſams vpperis wißnotaļļ / 
Nhepatick töw / tu to apſmey / 
Tawas Atzis to eenied / 
Bett Deewa Vpperis gir tas / 
Weens ẜalauſietz Gharrs.
5. Weenu ẜalauſietu vnd ẜagrauſietu Ꞩirrdi / 
	Tu nhe mettieſẜi attpackaļļ / 
	Vnd to nhe apſmeeſẜi / 
	To warr es ghanne apdohmaht :/: 
O Kunx Deews darri labb Zionam / 
	Pehtz tawu labbu kraßnu Prahtu / 
	Jerusalem tohß Muhrus / 
	Tu attkall vsdarrieſẜi :
Tad buhs töw labbs Prahts vnd Preex / 
Par to Vpperi tahs Taißnibas / 
Tad töw pattix tee Dädſami=vpperi / 
Tad tohs labbus Teļļus / 
Vs tawu Altari Lix.

 @v{Von allen Menſchen abgewand.}
	NO wiſẜeems Czillwäkeems es noſkirrohß / vnnd mannu
	Dwehſẜel paczeļļu :/: Py töw ween O Kunx mans Deews / 
	Nhe laid man iſẜamiſt / Wiſẜa manna czerriba ſtahw vs töw / 
Nhe laid man kaunà pallickt / Ka manni Eenaidneeki nhe preezayahß.

	2. Nhe weens Kaunà nhe pallix / No teems kattri vs töw czerre
:/: Eekſchan tawahms Rohkahms tee drohſche eedt / Nhe buhß
teem ſchäl ta Preetze : Laid wiſẜi tee apſmeeti gir / kattri ļaun darra
taweems nabbageems / Beß Teeſẜu vnd beß wiſẜas Wainas.
	3. Radi man tawu czeļļu O Kunx / Tahs Pähdas vs töw man
mahzi :/: Eekſchan tawu Teeſẜibu man waddi / Aiſto tu es mans
@b{Deews}

[316.lpp.]
Deews vnd Kunx / Manna Peſtiſchana / mans Preex / Palliex vnd
Paddomadehwetays / vs kattru es allaſch paļauyohß / vnd allaſch
läppo vnd gräſcho.
	4. Apdohma mans Kunx Ꞩirrdige / vnde to apghada :/: Ko
tu taweems Titzigeems ſohliyis eſẜi / kattreems tu tawu ſchälaſtibu
dohd: No muhſchibas eſẜi tu tohs ißredſeyis / Paſẜarrgayis ar tawu
Paddomu / czaur kattru tee tohp ſwähti.
	5. Manno Behrnigu Nheẜappraſſchanu / vnd wiſẜu mannu
Parradu :/: Nhe peeminni O Kunx Deews / Bett tawas lehnibas
dehļ / Abſchäloyees jo par man / No wiſẜeems Ghräkeems man peſty
/ pehtz tawas Mylibas.
	6. Tas Kunx gir ẜalldäns vnd beß Willtu / Wiſẜeems kattri vs

ẜayems / Vnd mahzies teems ẜawu Prahtu / Raxtiedams eekſchan

	7. Wiſẜi czeļļi tha Kungha gir Patteeſẜiba / lehniba vnd tyhra

Kattri waiza pehtz wiņja Wahrdu / Vnd titz ko tas eekſchan to ẜohla

ſtundas /Tapehtz man tawu Wahrdu mahzi / Ka es to czeļļu warru

	9. Ta Czillwäka Dwehſſele kattra Deewu byſtahs / Wiņja 
Manntu dabbuis :/: Wiſẜi tee kattri tam titzädami pehtz ſtaiga /
Tee nhe taps ẜamaitati : Tas Kunx gir wiņjo paſlähptas Brunņas /
Ꞩawu Eeſtadiyumu taß teems attwehrt gribb / Vnde ẜawa gharru 
doht.
	10. Mannas Atzis allaſchien vs töw / O Kunx Deews vsgreeſuſſchees
:/: Ka tu man gribbätu palliedſeht no to Tieklu / Eekſchan 
katru es äßmu apmättenahtz : Abſchäloyees par man vnd vsraugi
man / Aiſto es äßmu nabbax / Vnd no wiſẜeems attſtahtz.
@b{11. Man-}

[317.lpp.]
	11. Mannas Ꞩirdtz ẜahpes gir daſchadas / No mannu Lixtu
man peſty :/: Vsluhko ka es nitzinahtz tohpu / No Mohkahms ghullu

	11. Paſẜarrgi mannu Dweſẜel / vnd ghelb mann / Ka es nhe

@v{Allein zu dir HERR JEſu CHriſt.}

	3. Dohd man pehtz tawas Schälaſtibas / to yhſtänu

mannu Tuwaku ka man paſſcham / Paſtarà ghallà tawu Palligu
man ẜuhti / ka peepeſch / tha Wälla Willtiba no man greeſchahs.

	4. Ghohdtz gir Deewam auxtibà / tam Tähwam wiſẜas leh@b{nibas
:/:}

[318.lpp.]
nibas :/: Vnd JEſu CHriſto wiņja mylighakam Dählam / katters
mums allaſch paghlabbo : Vnd Deewam tam ſwähtam Gharram

@v{O CHriſte	Morgenſterne.}
		O CHriſte Rytasſwaigsne / ſpied mums ar ſpohſchu Ghaiſmu
/ Apghaißmo mums no Däbbäſẜu / ſchinny tumbẜà weeta
/ Ar tawu deewiſku Wahrdu.
	2. O JEſu Preex tho Nabbago / Manna Ꞩirdtz dohma vs
töw / Tu abſchäloſẜees töw par man / tawu ſchälaſtibu man dohſẜi / 
to titzu es töw no Ꞩirdtz.
	3. Es nhe warru neds ghribbu ghulleht / Es nhe warru preeziex

Mohkams / O CHriſte abſchäloyeeß par man.
	4. O JEſu mans myļais Kunx / tu weeniex Deewa Dähls / 
No Ꞩirdtz es töw ghribbu / tu man ſchehlige palliedſi / Tu eſẜi tahs
ſchälaſtibas Krähßlis. 
	5. Tu eſẜi mannis dehļ ißlehyis / tawu ẜarrkannu Aſẜini / Laid to
par labbu man notickt / Eepreezini man czaur tawu Lehnibu / Palliedſi
man / to eß töw luhdſchu.
	6. Gir töw tick ļohte ẜaſẜiſta / Tawa nabbaga Dwehſẜele / Tad
attgreeſees tu ẜöw py mann / Es ghribbu taws Palliex buht / vnd 
peedohd Parradu vnd Nopällnu.
	7. Atſtayees tu wiſchkim no Ghräkeems / vnd eſẜi weens labbs
Czillwähx / Es gribbu patz töw myļoht / Vnd doht mannu gharru / 
Tam buhß töw to Däbbäſẜu rahdiet. 
	8. Es ghribbu patz töw meeloht / Ar mannu Meeſẜu vnd Aſẜini
/ Mannu Myläſtibu töw parrahdiet / vnd ghribbu töw ißdalliet
Mannu Dahwanu vnd wiſẜu Baggatibu.
	9. O JESV ghohdu vnnd ſlawu / dſeedu es töw

[319.lpp.]
allaſchien / To Titzibu eekſchan man wayro / Ka es pehtz ſcho laiku /

@v{Mein Sünd ich beicht vnd klage.}
@v{Jm Thon:}
@v{HErr CHriſti der einig GOttes Sohn.}
	MAnnus Ghräkus es attſiſtu vnd ſuhdſcho / Ar kattreems es
	töw mans Deews :/: Apkaitenayis äßmu wiſẜu manno muhſcho
/ Vnd ghanne nopellniyis to Nahwu : Tomähr kad tee
man no Ꞩirdtz / Schäli gir / vnd ruhp ghauſche / Peedohd maan 
Kunx ſchehlige. 
	2. Bett to luhdſchu es töw Deews / czaur CHriſtum tawu Dählu
/ Katters par mums gir czeetis / vnd muhſẜo Ghräko Parradu / 
Py Kruſtu gir nomaxayis / czaur ẜawu Mirrſchanu mums wiſẜeems /
Nopirzis to muhſchigu Krohni.
	3. Tapehtz O ſchehlighais Deews / Nhe vsluhko muhſẜus 
Ghräkus :/: Bett wiſẜe wairahk CHriſtum / Katters par mums 
ghir ghanne darriyis / Vnd ſöw py Krußtu lickahß nokauteeß / Apmehditeeß
vnd neewatees / Tas ſkieſts nhenoſeedſiex Jährs.

@v{O CHriſte wahrer GOttes Sohn.}
@l{Primi toni,}
O Chriſte patteeſẜe Deewa dähls Muhſchiga Tähwa ghiemis eſẜi.
@b{O Chri-}

[320.lpp.]
	O CHriſte patteeſẜe Deewa Dähls / Muhſchiga Tähwa
	ghiemis eſẜi.
		Czaur tawu Nopällnu mums gir dalliba / Tahs dſiewibas
vnd ſchälaſtibas.
	Vsraugi man tock O myļais Deews / Ar Ghräko Naßtu apgrutenatu
ghauſche.
	O myļais Kunx es luhdſchu vsraugi / Ar taweems Atzeems / 
vnd mannis ẜaugi.
	Kattrus tu weenkahrt ghreeſi vs to / Kaß töw aißleedſe ẜawu 
Kunghu.
	Tawas ſchehligas Atzis attgrees vs man / Ka tu darriyi tai
Ꞩeewinyai.
	Kattra ẜawus Ghräkus no Ꞩirdtz ẜuhdſeya / Tawas Kayas
ar Aſẜarams maſghaya.
	Vnd ar teems Matteems noſchaweya / Aran myläſtibu dauds
kahrt töw ſkuhpſtiya.
	Parradi / O Kunx / mann tawu Waigu / Lieds ka tu redſeyi
vs to mylige.
	Katters ar leelu Ghräko Naßtu / Töw ẜahnohß karraya py
to Kruſtu. 
	Vsraugi mannus Ghräkus vnd Noſegummu / kattri eekſchan
Elles man noſtumm.
	Aiſto beß töw nhe gir nhe weens / Kas man klaht ſtahw vnd
man pallieds.
	Es äßmu / way mannim / Ghräkoyis dauds / Manni Ghräki
ghull vs mann ghauſche.
	To paſſcho gir wairahk nhe ka Ꞩmilltis / kattri attraßti tohp
py Juhres mallis.
	Bett czaur tawu Spähku gir ẜalauſta / To Ghräko vnd Noſeedſibas
Wallſte.
	Tu weens to nabbago Palliex eſẜi / To paſſcho töw abſchäloyees.

@b{Aiſto}

[321.lpp.]
Aiſto ka tu Kunx JEſu CHriſt / To Ghrähzeneeko Palliex 
eſẜi. 
Tapehtz rahdi man tawu ſpehzigu Rohku / Palliedſi man warren
vnde ļohte.
Ka es mannus Ghräkus ar Peteri ẜuhdſchu / Py töw attgreeſchohß
vnd töw peeluhdſchu.
Vnd ar to nabbagu Ghräzeeneeß / Töw myļoht eeẜaku no
Ꞩirdtz.
Vnd preekſchan töw warru paſtaweht / Vnd eekſchan Däbbäẜẜu
warru ee=eedt.
Kattru tu redſeht licki / Tam Släppkawam turr muhſchige.
Czaur tawu czeſchanu vnd Nhawu ruhkt / laid man no Ghräkeems
nhemaitatam kluht.
Bett laid mannai Ꞩirrdei attraſt / Ka es ſkieſts äßmu no Ghräko
naßtu.
O Deews mans Kunx paklauſẜi man / laid meerige mirrt tawam
Kallpam.
Attpeßti mannu Dwehſẜel no Elles ẜahpes / Palliedſi ka es eekſchan
Däbbäſẜu nahku.
Ghohdtz gir tam Tähwam vnd tam Dählam / Vnd tam ſwähtam
Gharram.
Ka no Eeẜakumu gir biyis / Vnd palleek muhſcho muhſchohß / 
Amen.

XIX.
@v{Von der Rechtfertigung.}
@v{Durch Adams Fall iſt gantz verderbt.}
CZaur Adama Ghräkeems wiß gir ẜamaitahtz / Czillwehziga 
Eyembſchana vnd peedſimbſchana :/: Tee paſſchi Ghräki 
@b{mums}

[322.lpp.]
mums eedſimbti gir / no teems mehs nhe warram / peſtiti tapt / beß 
Deewa Dählu kas mums peſtyis gir / no tahdu leelu Wainu / kad
ta Tſchuhßka ſawu parrunnaya / Deewa dußmibu vs ẜöw rautees.
2. Ka tad nu ta Tſchuhßka Eewu gir parrunnayuſẜi / Ka ta
gir parkapuſẜi :/: Deewa Wahrdu / to nitzinadama / Ar to vs mums
wiſẜeems / Rawuſẜi gir to Nawu / tad by jo wayag / Ka Deewam
arridſan by mums dohdt / ẜauwu myļu Dählu to Peßtitayu / czaur
kattru mehs warrätam dſiewoht. 
3. Ka mums nu gir ſweſſchi Ghräki / Eekſchan Adamu wiẜẜeems
Kaunu darriyuſchi :/: Ta gir mums ſweſſcha ſchälaſtiba / Eekſchan
CHriſto wiſẜus ſaliedſenayuſẜi / Vnd ka mehs wiſẜi czaur Adama
noſegumu / äſẜam muhſchigà Naweh nomirruſchi / Ta gir Deews
czaur Chriſti Nawu / Atjaunayis kas by ẜamaitahtz.
4. Tas gir mums ẜawu Dählu dehwis / Kad mehs wehl
wiņja Eenaidneek biyam :/: Katters par mums py Kruſta pakahrtz / 
Nokautz / eekſchan Däbbäſẜu brautzis gir / czaur to mehs äſẜam / no
Nawes vnd Mohkam Peſtiti ja mehs pallaiſchamees / vs ſcho Preeku
/ ta Tähwa Wahrdu / kam ghribb to Mirrſchano dehļ ſchauſſchalas
par=eedt?
5. Tas gir tas czellſch / ghaiſchums / tee Wahrti / Ta Taißniba 
vnd ta Dſiewiba :/: Ta Tähwa paddoms / vnd muhſchiex Wahrdtz / 
kattru tas mums gir dehwis / Par weenu Ꞩarrgu / ka mehs ar drohſchu
Ꞩirrdi Tam warram ſtippre titzeht / Tapehtz mums nhe tick
dries / Nhe weens ſpähx neds Warra / No wiņja Rohkams ißrauß.
6. Tas Czillwähx gir beßdeewiex vnd nolahdehtz / Wiņja Peſtiſchana
gir arridſan wehl tahļe :/: Kas Preeku py Czillwäku meckle
/ Vnd nhe py Deewu to Kunghu : Aiſto kaß ghribb czittu czeļļu / 
beß ſcho Eepreezetayu ſtaigaht / To warr ghann dries ta Wälla
Spähx / ar ẜawu Willtibu ißbeedenaht. 
7. Kas Deewam titz / vnd vs to pallaiſchahs / Tas muhſcham
nhe tohp Kaunà :/: Aiſto kas vs ſcho Ackmini ſtahw / Jeb tam arridſan
vseedt dauds Nhelaimes / tomähr es muhſcham / nhe äßmu 
@b{to Czill-}

[323.lpp.]
Czillwäku redſeyis krietam / katters ẜöw palaiſchahß vs Deewa
Wahrdu / Tas pallieds wiſẜeems ẜaweems Titzigeems.
8. Es luhdſcho / O Kunx / no Ꞩirdtz dibben / tu nhe ghribbätu
no man attjembt :/: Tawu ſwähtu Wahrdu no mannas Muttes / 
tad man nhe apkaunehß / Manni Ghräki vnd Noſegumi / vs tawu
ſchälaſtibu es wißkim paļļauyohß / kas nu ſtippre vs to pallaiſchahß
/ Tas nhe byhẜees par to Mirrſchanu.
9. Manneems Kahjeems gir taws ſwähtz Wahrdtz / weena eedädſenata
Ꞩwetze :/: Ghaiſchums katters man to czeļļu rahda / ja
schi Rytas=ſwaigsne Eekſchan man vslätz tudeļļ ẜapproht / Tas
Czillwähx to leelu Dawanu / kattru Deewa Gharrs teems teeſcham
ẜohly / kattri vs to czerre.

@v{Es iſt das Heyl vns kommen her.}
TA Peſtiſchana gir mums nahkuſẜi / no tyru ſchälaſtibu vnnd

dſiewoht : Ta gir tas weens ſpohſch Speegels / katters mums
parrada to ghrezigu dabbu / eekſchan muhſẜu Meeſẜu apſläptu.

attſtahta tapt :/: Vnd jeb tas daſchkahrt baudietz tappa / Tomähr
tee Ghräki wairahk czehlehß : Ta Willteneeka darrbu Deews ļohte
nolahd / Vnd tai Meeſẜy tee Ghräki / allaſchien palleek peedſimbti.
@b{5. Tomähr}

[324.lpp.]

tas peepiildiyis / Ar to ẜawa Tähwa Dußmibu kluſẜenayis / kattras
par mums wiſẜeems ghaya.

par Dſiewibu buht / Tu eſẜi preekſchan man maxayis.

nhe mäloſẜi / Kas titz eekſchan man / vnd tohp Chriſtietz / Tam gir ta 
Debbes attpirckta / Ka tas nhe taptu paſuſts.

:/: Ta Titziba czaur to atſpied / Ja ta tohß darrbus nhe leeds /

labb / Eſẜi tu no Deewu peedſimmis.

[337.lpp.]

par jums apſchälotees / Nhe kahtz Ahrſts tam Wäſẜälam gir wayage
/ Wiņjo Darrbs tohp par ſmeeklu.
	8. Kad tu warrätohß ẜöw ko nopellnitees / Kapehtz by tad wayaga
man par töw nomirrth / Schiß ghalldz töw arridſan nhe pallieds
/ Ja tu ẜöw paſſcham pallidſeht ghribbi.
	9. Titzi tu to no Ꞩirrdtz dibben / atſieſti ar to Mutt /tad eſẜi tu
labbe vnd pareiſe ghattaws / Vnd ta Barriba tawu Dweſẜel eepreezina.

	10. Teems Augļeems nhe buhß arridſan ißpallieckt / Tawu Tuwaku
buhß töw myļoht / Ka tu tam pallidſeht warr / Jhten ka taws
Deews py töw dariyis gir.

@v{GOtt ſey gelobet vnd gebenedeyet.}
		DEwam mehs ſlawejam vnd ẜackam patteitzibu Aiſto wings
		mums patz gir meelohyis :/: Ar ẜawu Meeſẜu vnd ar ẜawu
		Aſẜini / to leetz Kunx Deews mums par labbu notickt / Kyrie
eleiſon.
	2. Kunx czaur tawu ſwähtu Meeſſu / kattra no tawu Maht
Maria nahze / Vnd tas ſwähtz Aſẜins / Pallieds Kunx mums no
wiſẜams bähdams / Kyrie eleiſon.
	3. Ta ſwähta Meeſẜa gir par mums nodohta / Eekſchan Nahwu
/ ka mehs czaur to warrätam dſiewoht :/: Nhe leelaku{leekaku} ſchälaſtibu
warrätu tas mums dahwenaht / Py kattru mumsto by peeminneht
/ Kyrie eleiſon.
	4. Kunx tawa leela Myläſtiba töw ſpeeduſẜi gir / Ka tawam
Aſẜinim py mums by leelu brienumu darrieth / vnd nomaxaht muhſẜu
Parradu / Ka nu Deews attkal muhſẜu Draux gir tappis / Kyrie
eleiſon.
	5. Deews dohd mums wiſẜeems ẜawu ſcheligu Swähtumu / ka mehs
eetam vs ẜaweems czeļļeems / eekſchan ihſtänu Myläſtibu / vnd brahligu
Peetitzibu / Ka mums ta Barriba nhe ähd to Ꞩirrdi / Kyrie eleiſ.
@b{6. Kunx}

[338.lpp.]
	6. Kunx tawu ſwähtu Gharru muhſcham nhe attjemm no 
mums / katters mums mahza turreht patteeſẜu Titzibu / ka tawa
nabbaga Chriſtita Draudſiba / dſiewo eekſchan Meeru vnd Weenaidibu
/ Kyrie eleiſon.

@v{Collecten nach der Communion.}
Deews Kunx gir ar jums. Antwort:
Mums noteek pehtz tawu Wahrdu.
Laideta mums Deewam patteickt:
	O Patteeſẜe Deews / wiſẜewalldyx Tähws / mehs 
	luhdſam töw no Ꞩirdtz dibben / leetz mums nabbageems
to Auglu vnd Dahwanu tahs ſwähtas 
Mohzibas muhſẜa Kungha JEſu CHriſti / tas gir / to 
ſchälaſtibu vnd Ghräko Pammeſſchanu ar titzigu Ꞩirrdi
ſtippre ẜayembt / ka mehs pehtz tawa myļa Dähla 
Wahrdu / wiņja ſwähtu Meeſẜu vnd dahrgu Aſẜini / kattru
tas par mums nodehwis vnd ißlehyis gir / ar to
Maiß vnd Wynu patteſẜe äſẜam jämuſchi / czaur to paſſchu
tawu myļu Dählu muhſẜu Kunghu JEſum Chriſtum
/ katters ar töw vnd to ſwähtu Gharru dſiewo vnd 
wallda pattees Deews allaſchien vnd muhſchige / Amen.

@v{Ein ander.}
	OCh tu myļais Kunx vnd Deews / katters tu py
	ſcho briniſku Wackarehden tawu Mohzibu peeminneht
vnd mahziet mums pawehleyis eſẜi:
@b{Dohd}

[339.lpp.]
Dohd mums / Ka mehs to paſſchu tawu Meeſẜu vnd Aſẜini
tha warram wallkoht / ka mehs tawu Labbu darriſchanu
ick deenas eekſchan mums nomannyht warram

vnd walldi / pattees Deews allaſchien vnd muhſchige
/ Amen.

@v{Ein anders.}

@v{Ein anders.}

@b{Kunx}

Swähtz gir muhſẜu Deews / 
Swähtz gir muhſẜu Deews / tas Kunx Zebaoth. 
Tawa Deewiſka Warra vnd Ghohdiba / 
Eedt par Debbes vnd Semmes tahļe. 
To ſwähto Apuſtuļļo Draudſiba / vnd wiſẜi myļi Proweetes.

Ta wiſẜa Chriſtita draudſiba / Teitz töw wirſẜon Semmes allaſchien.

	weenigu Dählu.

Tu Konings tas ghodibas JEſu CHriſt / Deewa Tähwa muhſchiex
Dähls tu eſẜi.

Tu ſehd py Deewa labbas Rohkas / Ar wiſẜu ghohdu eekſchan Tähwa
Wallſtibas.

Kattri ar tawu dahrgu Aſẜini attpeſtiti gir.
Laid mums Debbeſẜiehß dallibai buht /

@v{Dich O GOTT loben wir.}

ta Tähwa. 
Mehs titzam töw / tu no turrenes attnaxi weens Ꞩohgis.

Pallidſi mums / kattrus tu atpirrzis eſẜi / ar tawu dahrgu Aſẜini.

Tu ghribbätu / O Kunx / mums ickdeenas / no Ghräkeems jo paſẜarghat.

tapt : Tawas lehnibas dehļ / O ſchehliex Deews / Hallelujah.

par wiß / Peſti mums arridſan no wiſẜu Nhelaimibu / Tahs Meeſẜas

@v{Was Lobes ſolln wir dir O Vater ſingen?}

XXII.
@v{Vom Chriſtlichen Leben vnd Wandel.}
@v{Kompt her zu mir ſpricht GOttes Sohn.}
@b{Nahzeeta}

[349.lpp.]
		NAhzeeta ſchurr py man / ẜacka Deewa / Dähls / Wiſẜi / kattri
		juhs eſẜeeta abghrutenati / No Ghräkeems ļoht nomahkti /

jums doht / kas mann gir / ghribbu dſeedenaht juhſẜu Wainu.
	2. Manna Juhga gir ẜalldäna / manna naßta gir weegla / Kaß
to mann labpraht pehtz näß / To Ell tas ißbehx / Es ghribbu tam
teeſcham pallidſeht neſt / Ar mannu Palligu tas panahx / To muhſchigu
Däbbäſẜu Wallſtibu.
	3. Ko eß äßmu darriyis vnd ſcheitan czeetis / Dſiewodams wähle
vnd aggre / To buhß jums arridſan darriet: Ko juhß domayeeta / 
runnayeeta vnd darraita / Tas gir wiß labbs vnde pareiſe / Kad taß
noteek pehtz Deewa Prahtu.

ja=czeeſch : Nu nhe warr tas jo czittahde buht / Tapehtz eedohdeeß ar 
labbu Prahtu / Ja tu ghribbi muhſchigas Mohkas ißbehkt.
	5. Wiſſa raddita leeta dohd leezibu / kas dſiewo eekſchan Vhdeni

ẜamaitatay tapt.

czittz ſtrahda to / czittz ſtrahda ſcho / Ꞩawu nabbagu Dwehſẜel 
taß wißkim aismirſẜa / dſiewodams wirſẜon Semmes.

ka Deewa ſchläſtiba / kattru wings allaſch nitzinayis gir / Nhe lähte
par to nahx.

:/: Tad Deews dries attrohdahß / Sawa ſpähku vnd Schälaſtibu

Kaunu / no Kehdehms vnd no Ꞩaitehms / ta lieds arridſan no
Nahwes.
	3. Vs to ghribbu es paļļautees / mannà ghruhtà laikà :/: Tas
mann nhe buhß ſchähl / Wings noghreeſch wiſẜu ļaun : Es tam wißſkim
pawehlu / Mannu Meeſẜu / mannu Dwehſẜel / mannu dſiewibu
/ Wiß gir Deewam padohta / Wings warr darrieth / Ka tam
pattiek. 
	4. Tas ween wiņjam pattiek / Kas mann wayaga gir :/: Wings
myļo mums no Ꞩirdtz dibben / dohd mums to Kunghu CHriſt / Ja
ẜawu myļu Dählu: / czaur to wings mums ee=dahwena / Kas Meeß
vnd Dweſẜel warr vsturreht / Slahweyeeta to Debbeſẜys.
	5. Slahweyeeta to ar Ꞩirrdi vnd Mutt / wings abbediwi
mums dohd :/: Tha gir ſwähta ſtunda / eekſchan kattras mehs wiņju
eeghadayam / czittz laix wiß ißniext / eekſchan kattru mehs dſiewoyam
/ mums buhß ſwähteems tapt / vnd pallickt muhſchige.
	6. Jeb ta Paſẜaule ißniext / ar ẜawu leppnibu vnd Ghreſnibu :/: 
Neds Ghohdiba vnd Mannta palleek / Ta by pirmahk auxta:
Mehs tohpam nomirruſchi / dſiļļi Semme ee=rackti / kad mehs ghulleyuſchi
äſẜam / ghribb Deews mums Vsmohdenaht.
	7. Ta Dweſẜele nhe paſuhd / wäßta eekſchan Abrahams Klehpi
:/: Ta Meeſẜa tohp jauna peedſimbta / beß wiſẜeems Ghräkeems /  
wiſkim ſwähta / vnd ſkieſta / Weens Bährns vnd Mannteeneex tha
Kungha / To mums czittahd nhe pahr=runnahß / taß Wälls ar ẜawu
Willtibu.
	8. Tapetz jeb es ſcheitan czeeſchu / Nhelaimibu vnd Mohkas :/: 
Ka es tohs ghann nopällnu / tomähr nahk muhſchiex laix / Gir pills
Preezibas / Tho patti beß wiſẜas mitteſchanas / ka es CHriſtum atſieſtu
/ mann buhß redſeht vnd juſt.
	9. Tas gir Deewa Tähwa Prahtz / katters mums raddiyis
@b{gir :/:}

[357.lpp.]
gir :/: Wiņja Dählam gir dauds labbumu / Schälaſtibu tas mums 
nopellniyis gir: Arridſan Deews tas ſwähtais Gharrs / Eekſchan
Titzibas tas mums wallda / Eekſchan Däbbäſẜa=wallſtibas tas 
mums wadda / Tam mehs patteitzam.

@v{O Menſch wolleſt bedencken.}
O Tu Czillwähx apdohma / Mannu leelu ruhktu Mohku :/: 
Es ghribbu töw attkal dahwenaht / To dſiewibu par to Nawu
/ Py man buhs töw thurreteeß / Es äßmu töw par labbe
/ To Däbbäſẜu attwehris. 
2. Es nhe äßmu töw attneſẜis / czaur Ꞩuddrabbu vnd Sälltu :/: 
Ar mannu Aſẜini nomaxayis / Ka eſẜi tu tad tick läppnis? Wirſẜon
Semmes Manntu ẜakraht / czaur to tawu Dwehſẜel ẜamaitaht / arrieg
es töw to mahziyu?
3. Kas ſcheitan to Baggatibu eeghribbahs / Par mannu Lehnibu
:/: To buhß tay Ruhſẜei ẜamaitaht / vnd buht tam muhſchige 
ſchähl : Ꞩackrahtu eekſchan Däbbäſẜu / Tur juhß attraſẜeeta to leetu
/ Kaß jums py Dwehſẜeles wayaga gir.
4. Tee Pugki wirſẜon to Lauku / ka krahßne tee turr ſtahw :/: 
Tee nhe maxa ar Naudu / To Krahßnumu / kattra teems gir : Salomons
ẜawahß Drehbehß / Nhe by lieds weenai lappai / To paſſcho
Pugkiņjo.
5. Tee Puttninyi appackſchan Debbeß / gir liexmi ẜawà lißdà :/: 
Tahs Lapſas ẜawà Allà / Tohp no mann paſẜarghatas / Es nhe äßmu
nheneeka patturreyeeß / Vs ko es ẜawu ghallwu lieckt warru / 
Kas kaitas gir tad mann nu ?
6. Debbes vnd Semme mann peedärr / Wiß Krahßnums arridſan
klaht :/: Kas ghribb tad mann mannus Ļaudis ißwillt / Kattrus
es äßmu weddis / Aran Egyptero Semmes / Ar ẜawu ſtippru
Rohku / Eekſchan tahs ẜohlitas Semmes.
7. Tapehtz nhe bähdayeeteeß / Kattri juhß manni Mahzekļi eſẜeeta
:/: Par Barribu neds par Drehbems / Es ghadayu par jums / 
@b{Es}

[358.lpp.]
Es ghribbu jums wiſẜus barryoht / Par Auxtumu / Baddu Paſẜargaht
/ To titzeeta mann patteeſẜe.
8. Tad eſẜeeta nu ar Meeru / Ar to Allgu kattra jums kļuhſt :/: 
Mans Tähws jums allaſchien dohß / Wiß kas jums wayaga gir / 
Ka juhß nhe iſẜamiſẜaht / Kad jums paſtarà Deenà / Preekſchan ta
Czillwäka Dählu jaſtahw.
9. Ghohtz / ſlawa vnd Patteitziba / Gir Deewam ẜatzita muhſchige
:/: Par ẜawu jauku Mahzibu / Kattru tas mums gir ẜattaiſſiyis
/ Ar ẜawu Deewiſku Mutt / Taß pallieds wiſẜahs Stundahs / 
Eekſchan Däbäſẜu=wallſtibas.

@v{Jch weiß mir ein Blümlein iſt hübſch vnd fein.}
ES ſinnohß ẜöw weenu Pugkiet / ta gir jauka vnd ſkaiſta / 
Ta gir man pa Pratam / Ta patiek eekſchan mannu Ꞩirrdi / 
Ta patti Pugkite / par wiſẜeems czitteems Pugkitems.
2. Ta Pugkite gir tas Deewa Wahrdtz / Kattru Deews mums
gir dehwis / Tas wädd mums vs to ſchauru czeļļu / ſcheit vnd turr / 
Eekſchan tahs muhſchigas dſiewoſchanas. 
3. Tas gir tas czellſch / tas ghaiſchums / tee Wahrti / Ta
Taißniba vnd ta Dſiewiba / Kas ẜawo Ghräko dehļ bähdayahß / 
vnd no teems attſtahy / Tam gir tee czaur CHriſtum peedohti.
4. Tas ẜacka : nahzeeta ſchurr wiſẜi py mann / Wiſẜi kattreems
ta Ꞩirrdtz gir ghruta / Es ghribbu ka juhs paſſchi ghribbaht / to titzaht
/ Dſeedenaht juhſẜu Wainu.
5. Jemmeeta / ähdeeta / ta gir manna Meeſẜa / Kattru taggad
es jums dohmu / Es dahwenu jums wiſẜu mannu Manntu / Ka
juhs warreeta mannis peemineht.
6. Jemmeeta vnd dſerreeta tas gir mans Aſẜins / To äßmu
es juhſẜo dehļ ißleyis / Katters ghanne darra par juhſẜeems Ghräkeems
/ czeekahrt juhs to darraita / Ka es jums to äßmu eeſtadiyis.

@v{Lieb GOtt für allen dingen.}

@v{Was kan vns kommen an für Noht.}

@v{Da es wol gieng / mein Hertz vnd Sinn.}
@v{Jm Thon :}

Laime / neds Nhelaimiba / Mann muhſchige warrehs ſchaubiet.

@b{man}

@v{An Waſſer Flüſſen Babylon.}
PY Babyloņa Vhdens Straumes / Teitan ẜehdeyam mehs
bähdadameeß :/: Kad mehs domayam vs Zion / Tad raudayam

Kungham dſeedaht ẜawu dſeeßmu / tick ſweſſchà Semmeh : Jeruſa@b{lem}


[364.lpp.]
lem ja es töwis aiſmirſtu / Tad tas taißnis Deews / laid aismirrſt

mannai Mehlei peekehrteeß / Vnd py to Schohgli peelipt.

mannu Preeku vnd ſlawu / Taggadien vnd muhſchige :

ſtundas / Jßpohſty tohs lieds patt Dibbinam / To Pammatu ghribbam
mehs maitaht.
5. Tu ſkaudiga Meita Babylon / ẜalauſita vnd ißpohſtita :/:
labb tam / kas töw dohs ẜawu Allgu / Vnd töw attkal attmaxa / 
Tawu Pahrghallwibu vnd leelu blehdibu / Vnd mähro töw ar tahdu

Bährnus / Ꞩakamp vnd ſweeſch tohs py Ackmini / Ka tu tohpi 
aiſmirſta. 

@v{Mag Jch Vnglück nicht wiederſtahn.}
JA es nhe warru Nhelaimibai prett ſtahweht / Vnd ta Paſẜaule
mann eenied / Mannas labbas Titzibas dehļ :/: Tad
tomähr es to ſinnu / Ta gir manna ghuddriba / Deewa Lehniba
vnd ſchälaſtiba / To buhs teems man attſtaht : Deews nhe gir 
taļe / Maſu briedi / Tas ẜöw paſleppyahß / teekams tas nomahz / 
Kattri mann ẜawu Wahrdu ghribb aplaupiet.
2. Es ißtaiſẜu ka ghribbädams ẜawas lietas / wahgs buhdams / 
vnd kad Deews mann leek beedinaht :/: Tad tomähr es ſinnu / nheweena
Warra muhſcham palleek / taß gir wiß labbahx / Tam laizigam
buhß ißniekt : Ta muhſchiga baggatiba / darra drohſſchu Ꞩirrdi
/ py to es palleeku / nhe bähdadams nheneeku / Deews pallieds
man to Vswarreht.
3. Wiſſas leetas weenu briedi ſtahw / ẜackams Wahrdtz gir / 
Kunx JEſu CHriſt / Tu ſtahweſẜi mann py ẜahneem :/: Vnd redſeſẜi
vs mannu Nhelaimibu / Jht buhtu ta tawa / Kad tavs mann
@b{vsbrux :}

[365.lpp.]
vsbrux: Buhs mann to tad czeeſt / ſchinny laikà / Paſẜaule ka töw
pattiek / Deews gir mannas Brunņas / Tas mann ghanne pawaddies.


@v{Zu dir allein in dieſer Noht.}
TÖw ween ſchinnieß lelohs bähdohs / Mehs tawi Bährni peeẜautzam
:/: Vs töw / tu wiſẜo ſcheligais Deews / Stahw 
muhſẜu Preex vnd czerriba: Tu ghribbätu tawohs dußmohß / 
Tahs ſchälaſtibas attghadatees / vnd muhs wiſkim nhe ẜamaitaht.
2. Pilla blehdibas / Deewam ſchähl / gir ſchi Semme / Teems
Ghräkeems wiſkim paſẜadawuſẜees :/: Tomähr dauds labbi töw paſieſtami
/ Pehtz tawu Prahtu dſiewo : Aiſto tu tawu Baſnizu ſchiny
weetà / Töw eſẜi taiſẜiyees czaur tawu Wahrdu / Tahs nhe ghribbätu
tu aismirrſt. 
3. Tas leelais Pullx töw / Kunx / neezina / Pehtz tawu Wahrdu
nheneeka bähda :/: Jeb mehs ghribbätam ar muhſẜu Spähku / Nhe
warram mehs teems to aisleekt: Tomähr mehs vs töw czerreyam / tu
nhe lixi mums attmaxaht / Wiņjo blehdibu vnd Noſeedſibu.
4. Ar Ghrähkeems mehs arridſan apghrutenati äſẜam / Tee gir 
mums ſchähl mums Nabbageems :/: To ẜohdibu vnd Riext äſẜam
mehs pellniyuſchi / Bett tu par mums töw abſchäloyees: Jemm nohſt
no mums muhſẜus Noſegumus / Kattrus CHriſtus par mums gir 
attmaxayis / vnd ka weens Tähws mums pamahzi.
5. Tu nhe eſẜi nhe weenkahrt bes Palligu vnd Preeku / tawus Ļaudis
/ O Deews attſtayis :/: Jſraeli tu atpeſtiyis eſẜi / Juhry vs ẜauſẜu
czeļļu / Kad nhe neekahtz Palliex wairs ghaiditins by / czaur töw ween
tee Ļaudis peſtiti tappa / tas Waideneex nhe warreya teems kaiteht.
6. Tha nu arridſan nahtz mums Palliga / Kattri mehs äſẜam
bähdohs : Ka mehs nhe tohpam ar Sobini vnd Vgguni / Nokauti
ſchodeen jeb riethe : Ta Waida kattra gir rädſäta / Py Wiereems / 
py Ꞩeewahms / py maſeems Bährneems / Nhe laid mums wairahk
redſeht. 
@b{7. Schy}

[366.lpp.]
7. Schy Semme mums eedohta gir / Preekſch dauds Ꞩimteems
Ghaddeems :/: Ka tee tawu Wahrdu / O JEſu CHriſt / 
Teems Ļaudeems mahzitu. Bett tee gir wairahk meckleyuſchi / 
ẜawu paſſchu labbumu / ghohdu vnd Preeku / Töwis ghann mas
ohladami.
8. To eſẜi tu paczeeßdams tick illge / Kunx Deews warreyis paczeeſt
:/: Nun vsmohſti tu / vnd isbaidini mums / Ka mehs no bailu
iſẜatruhzeenayamees: Tawa Ꞩohdiba / Tähws / gir allaſch pareiſa
/ Mehs darram ka Bährni / kattri kullti tohp / Tee nhe ẜackahs
kapehtz.
9. Jaw ẜenn ſchi Allga nopellnita gir / Jhsſchim eſẜi tu ghaidiyis
:/: Ka tam ta kahdu briedi notickt by / Tapehtz gir dauds baſchiyuſſchees:
Ꞩcho Auku dauds gir paredſeyuſſchi / Tam buhs juſt kas
nhe ghribb titzeht / Ar kaunu vnd Wainaneems mahziteeß.
10. Kunx CHriſt ſchinnies leelohs bähdohs / Mehs töw no
Ꞩirrdtz peeẜautzam :/: Tawas nabbagas Awis labbe paſẜargi / Ka
tohs tee Willki nhe apry / Tawà ghlabbſchanà mehs Meeſẜu vnd 
Dwehſẜel / Ähkus / Manntu ar Ꞩeewams vnd Bährneems / Töw
ween tohs pawehleyam. 
12. Muhſſeems Kungeems dohd to Prahtu / Ka tee pareis no Ghräkeems
atſtayahs :/: Vnd dſiewo pehtz tawu Wahrdu / töw parr ghohdu
vnd ſlawu / Töw biedamees ghaddige dſiewo / No Ꞩirdtz dibben
ſkaiſte töw kallpo / Teeſẜu vnd Taißnibu ghlabbo.
3. Dauds tuhxtoſchi Ļaudis gir / Kattri no töw / O Deews / 
nhe dſirrd :/: Tohs nhe leetz illghake mulldeht / To czeļļu vs töw
teems mahzi / kurr taws Ghohtz nhe tohp mecklähtz / Turr arridſan
laime nhe gir ghaiditina / Turr vs töw nhe warr paļautees.
14. Ka mehs ſchinny laikà peſtiti tohpam / Leelus Kungus
vnd Wirrſẜeneekus pamohdini :/: Dohd Paddomu / Spähku / dohd
drohſchibu / Ka Prettibneex iſẜabyhſtahs : Kad mehs petz to jauku
Meeru / czaur tawu ſchälaſtibu dabbuyuſchi buhſẜim / Muhſchige
ghribbam mehs töw patteickt.
@b{15. Scho}

[367.lpp.]

@v{Wend ab deinen Zorn / lieber GOtt.}

to tahs Debbeſẜes Manteneekus / Ar töw dſiewoht.

@v{GOtt Vater in dem Himmelreich.}
DEews Tähws eekſchan Däbbäſẜa wallſtibas / Deews Dähls / 
ta lieds Deews ſwähtais Gharrs / Tu ſwähta Triaidiba
/ Weens weeniex Deews muhſchige / Vs tawu ẜoliſchanu
mehs luhdſam töw / Tu ghribbätu mums ſchehlige packlauſẜiet.
2. Ach myļais Deews muhſẜo ſchälo / Pehtz muhſẜu Nopällnu
nhe dohd mums Allgu / Abſchäloyees par mums czaur tawu lehnibu
/ Meeſẜu / ghohdu / vnd Manntu paſẜargi par Nhelaim / Eſẜi 
mums ſcheliex / vnd palliedſi mums Kunx / Nhe attſtah no taweems
Ļaudeems muhſchige. 
3. Paſẜargi mums no ta Wälla blehdibu / Ka tas mums nhe
warr peewillt / Nowehrs no mums wiņja dedſigu bulltu / Palliedſi 
ka tas mums nhe vseedt peepehſch / Ach myļais Deews nhe attſtah
mums / Kad mums ta ļaune Paſẜaule kahrdina.
4. Paſẜargi mums Deews wiſẜà ſtundà / Par Apalloſchanu / 
Kaunu vnd Ghräku / Par Karryu / Eenaidibu vnd Dußmibu / Par
Vhdens / Vgguns=ghräku / vnd dahrgu laiku / Par Mehri vnd 
@b{peepehſchu}

[372.lpp.]
peepehſchu nheweſẜelibu / Par nicknu Auku vnnd leelu Wähtru.
	5. Paſẜargi mums Kunx wiſẜahs bähdahs / Jrr par ļaunu peepehſchu
Nahwu: Wiß wairahk Kunx nhe attſtah tad no mums / kad
mehs nahkam preekſchan tawu ẜohdibu / vnd par to muhſchigu Nahwu
/ Ock myļais Deews mums arridſan paſẜargi.
	6. Mehs nabbagi Ghräzeneeki wehl luhdſam / O JEſu CHriſte
myļais Kunx / Palliedſi mums czaur tawu ſwähtu Peedſimbſchanu
/ czaur to ſwähtu vsczellſchanu vnd Däbbäſẜies kahpſchanu / czaur

Aſẜinigu ſweedru / vnd ruhktu Nahwu.

to Wahrdu dohd tawu Gharru vnd ſpähku / Ka tas augļus näß / 
vnd py mums peeliep. 
	8. Titzigus Mahzetayus taweems Ļaudeems ẜuhti / Nhepatteeſẜu
mahzibu nowehrs no mums / Jßdellde wiſẜenadu willtibu / vnd 
wiſẜai Abgräzibai prettieb ſtahw / Jrr kattri wehl allotohs attgrees / 
vnd waddi tohs vs to taißnu czeļļu.
	9. Arridſan maita czaur tawu ſpehzigu Rohku / Kattri tawam
wahrdam prettie ſtahw / vnd preekſchan ta Kreewa ſpähku / Tawu
Wallſtibu nabbagu Pullku paſẜarrgi / Kattram ſcheit czeeſt buhs
wirſẜon Semmes / To Aſẜins preekſchan töw gir dahrx.
	10. Paglabbo arridſan muhſẜu Meeſẜu vnd Manntu / Noghres
wiſẜu Dumpi / Karryu vnd Aſẜino ißleeſchanu / Teems Koninyeems / 
vnd leeleems Kungeems / dohd ſchälaſtibu / ka tee pareiſe wallda / ka tee
arridſan Meeru turr / Ꞩarrghadamees par Eenaidibu vnd Karryu.

wiņjo Eenaidneeko ſpähku vnd Willtu / Paghlabbo arridſan

Pili / Rahtes Kungus / vnd wiſẜus Ļaudis / Tohs wiſẜus ghribbatu
tu paſẜarrghat.
@b{12. Wiſ-}

[373.lpp.]
12 . Wiſẜeems Chriſtiteems ẜawà Nhelaimibà / Nahtz palliga / 
tohs allaſch paghlabbo / Eepreezini vnd vsturri tohs Ꞩirrdes / kattras
ghrutas gir no leeleems bähdeems / Tohs bariņus ghellb / ar tawu
Rohku / Tahs Attraitnes vnd wiſẜus behdigus eepreezini.
13. Tahs Siedenatayas vnd wiſẜas abghrutenatas / Jrr Bährnus
paſẜargi par Nhelaim / Palliedſi wiſẜeems kattri wayi vnd Nhewäſſäli
gir / Ka wiņjo czerriba no töw nhe mitteyahs / darri wiņjo Dwehſẜeles
wäſẜälus / Vnd eepreezini tohs paſtarà ſtundà.
14. Deews Tähws tahs ſchälaſtibas / Ar taweems Engeliſcheems
pawaddi / Tahs Laiwes{Ļaiwes} / vnd wiſẜus czeļļa Ļaudis / Palliedſi
ka teems allaſch labb klayahs / Par wiſẜu Nhelaim / breeßmibu vnd 
bähdams / thos allaſchien ſchehlige paſſargi.
15. Ock myļais Kunx dohd ſtippri paczeeſt / Kattri beß wainas
ļaunu czeeſch / vnd peſti tohs no to Eenaidneeko Rohkams / Wiņjo
bähdas vnd czeetumu pahrwehrs / Eepreezini tohs arridſan paſtarahs
bähdahs / Kattri tohp wäßti vs Nahwes.

XXIV
@v{Von der Chriſtlichen Kirchen.}

tohs czaur tawu muhſchigu Spähku.

ghallam py töw palleekam / Laid ta Paſẜaule allaſch kurrne.

@v{O HERRE GOtt dein Göttlich.}
O Kunx Deews / Taws Deewiſkis Wahrdtz / Gir illge aptumſẜohtz
pallitzis :/: Kamährt czaur tawu lehnibu / Mums
gir ẜatzietz / Ko Paulus gir raxtiyiß / Vnde czitti / Apuſtuļi
wehl / czaur tawu Deewiſku Mutt / Par to patteitzam mehs / no
Ꞩirdtz ka mehs / peedſiwoyuſchi äſẜam to ſtundu.
2. Ka tas ar warru Preekſcha gir nahzis / ka mehs ar Atzims rädſam
:/: Ock Kunx mans Deews / abſchäloyees par teems / Kattri töw
wehl taggad aisleeds: Vnd wairahk dohdahs / vs Czillwezigu Mahzibu
/ Ar kattru tee tock ẜamaitayahs / Tawu Wahrdu ẜappraſt / dohd
teems O Deews / ka tee jo muhſcham nhe mirrſt.
3. Ghribbi tu nu krahßne / labbs Chriſtietz Czillwähx buht / Tad
buhß töw pirrmahk titzeht :/: Vs to pallaidees / Vnd leetz ſtippre
ſtahweht / czerribu vnd mylibu titzädams / Vs JEſum CHriſtum
ween / Allaſchien / tawu Tuwaku arridſan myļo / to meerigu Dwehſẜel
/ ſkieſtu Ꞩirrdi klaht / Nhe weena raddita leeta warr doht.
4. Bett töw / Kunx / weenam / buhs to darriet / No tyras lehnibas
:/: Kas ar to eepreezayahs / Tas gir peſtietz / Vnd nhe weens
tam nhe warr kaiteht : Jeb gribbätu ghanne / Muhki vnd wiſẜa Paſẜaule
/ Tohs vnd tawu Wahrdu ißdelldeht / Tomähr gir wiņjo ſpähx
Preekſchan töw weeni ſmeekli / Teem buhs to ghann ar meeru atſtaht.

@v{5. Kunx}

[383.lpp.]
5. Kunx Deews palliedſi / ſchinnyhs bähdahs / Ka tee ẜöw arridſan
atgreeſchahs :/: Kattri nhe neek apghada / Tawu Wahrdu
nitzina / Vnd nhe gribb arridſan mahzitees : Tee ta ween ẜacka / Tas
nhe gir tees / Vnd nhe gir to wehl laſẜiyuſchi / Neds muhſcham dſirdeyuſchi
/ Nhe gir ta paſẜcha Wälla buhsſchana.
6. Es titz to ſtippre / Ka tas gir tees / Ko Paulus gir vsraxtiyis
:/: Tas ta notix / Ka wiſẜas leetas ißniex / Bett taws Deewiex
Wahrdtz ween pallietz : Muhſchige / jeb tas ẜahpätu / dauds czeeteems
beßdeewigeems Ꞩirrdems / Ja tee nhe tohp labbaki / Buhß
teems tadehļ / czeeſt ļohte leelas ẜahpes.
7. Deews gir mans Kunx / Vnd es äßmu tas / kam tawa Mirrſchana
nahk par labb :/: Czaur to tu mums / No Ghräko Naßtu / 
Atpeſtiyis eſẜi ar tawu Aſẜini: Par to es töw patteitſchu / Tadehļ tu
mann / dohſẜi ko tu eſẜi ẜoliyis / Ko es töw luhdſcho{ļuhdſcho} / Nhe leeds mann
to / Jeb es dſiewo jeb mirrſtu. 
8. Kunx es czerre jo / Ka tu tadus / Nhe kahdas bähdahs attſtahſẜi
:/: Kattri tawu Wahrdu tees / Ka labbi Kallpi / No Ꞩirdtz
ar Titzibu ẜayämm : Dohd teems O Kunx / to ẜattaiſẜietu ſchälaſtibu
/ Vnd nhe leeds tohs ẜamaitaht / O Kunx czaur töw / Luhdſcho
es leetz mann / liexmige vnd labpraht nomirrth / Amen.

@v{Sie iſt mir lieb die werthe Magdt.}
ES czeeniyo to jauku Meitu / Vnd nhe warru tahs aismirrſt :/:
Slawa vnd Ghohtz no tahs tohp ẜatzietz / Ta gir mannu
Ꞩirrdi apmahneyuſẜi: Es myļo to / Jeb by mann arridſan / 
leelu Nhelaim czeeſt / Tomähr tas nhe kait / Ta gribb man atkal
eepreezenaht / Ar ẜawu mylibu prett mann / Kattru ta gribb ar mann
turreht / Vnd darriet wiß ko es ghribbu.
2. Ta näß no Sälltu tick ſkieſt weenu Krohni / Turr eekſchan
ſpied diwipadeßmitt ſwaigsnes :/: Wiņjas drehbes gir ſpohſchas ka
Ꞩaule / Tahs ſpied ſkaidre vnd tahļe : Vnd wirſẜon to Mehneß / 
wiņjas Kahyas ſtahw / Ta gir ta Bruhta / Tam Kungham iſẜohli@b{ta
/}

[384.lpp.]
ta / Tai gir ẜahpes / vnd buhs peedſimbt / weenu krahßnu Bährnu /

3. Tas darra tai wätzai Tſchuhßkai dußmuß / vnd gribb to

XXV.
@v{Jn Peſtilentz Zeiten / vnd Sterbensleufften.}
@v{Wer in dem Schutz des Höchſten iſt :}
@v{Jm Tohn:}
@v{Wo GOtt der HERR nicht bey vns helt:}
@v{Oder:}
@v{Auß tieffer Noht ſchrey ich zu dir.}
KAs ta Auxtaka Paglabboſchanà gir / Vnd Deeewam ẜöw
pawehleyahs :/: Tas ẜacka / Tu Kunx manns ghällbätaiß
eſẜi / Manna czerriba vnd manna dſiewiba: Katters tu mann
atpeſtieſẜi / No Wälla Wallgeems ſchälige / Vnd no Mehra trummeems.

2. Ar ẜaweems ſparneems wings töw apẜäds / Tam buhs töw 
paļautees :/: Wiņja Taißniba ghlabba töw ļohte / Ka töw Nacktieß
nhe kahda Breeßmiba / Neds Noſkumſchana ißbaideht warr / 
Neds kahda Bullta kattra py Deenu ſkrey / Tapehtz ka wiņja
Wahrdtz töw ſpied.
3. Nhe weens Mehris töw kaiteht warr / Katters nacktieß
@b{waſayahs :/:}

[385.lpp.]
waſayahs :/: Nhe kahda Nheweſẜeliba töw aiſkarr / Kattra deenas
widdu apſkraida : Jeb tuhxtohſchi mirrtu py taweem ẜahneem / Vnd
deßmittz=tuhxtohſchi pa labbu Rohku / Tomähr nhe buhs tam töw
aistickt.
4. Ja / tu arridſan tawas Ꞩirrdes Preeku / Ar taweems
Atzeems redſeſẜi :/: Py to Beßdeewigo Ꞩirrdeſẜahp / Kad Attmaxaſchana
notix : Kad tas Kunx tawa czerriba gir / Vnd tas Auxtakais
ẜawu ghlabboſchanu ẜohly / Tapehtz kad tu ẜöw tam paļauyees.
5. Nhe kahda Nhelaimiba töw notix / Nhe kahda Waina tawu
Nammu aiſkarrs :/: Aiſto tas Kunx ẜaweems Engeļeems allaſchien
/ Pawehļ töw labbe waddiet : Vnd töw paſẜarrgaht par ļaun / 
Vs Rohkams neſt wiſẜur / ka nhe kahtz Ackmins tawu Kahyu maita.
6. Vs Lahwehms / vnd Ohdſeems tu eeſẜi : Vnd mieſẜi vs
teems niekneems Tahrpeems :/: Vs jauneems Lawehms tu ſtahweſẜi
/ Wiņjo Sohbus apſmeedams : Aiſto nhe weens no teems töw
kaiteht warr / Nhe kada Ꞩehrga no czittu tam peelip / Katters vs
Deewu czerre. 
7. Tas eeghribbahs man no Ꞩirdtz dibben / Vnd czärre vs
mannu lehnibu :/: Tapehtz palliedſu es tam ick ſtundas / Es to
ghann ghribbu paſẜarrgaht : Es ghribbu allaſch wiņja Palliex buht / 
Tapehtz kad tas mannu Wahrdu paſieſt / Ar to buhs tam ẜöw
epreezateeß.
8. Tas peeẜautz man ka ẜawu Deewu / Tapehtz ghribbu es to 
paklauſẜiet :/: Es äßmu py to wiſſahs bähdahs / Es ghribbu tam palliedſeht
: Ghohdà es to ghribbu paczellt / Jllgu dſiewoſchanu es tam
ghribbu doht / Mannu Peſtiſchanu ghribbu es tam parahdiet.
9. Ghohtz gir tam Tähwam vnd tam Dählam / Vnd tam
ſwähtam Gharram :/: Ka no eeẜakumu by vnd nu / katters mums
ẜawu ſchälaſtibu parahda : Ka mehs ſtaigayam eekſchan wiņja czeļļu
/ Ka mums tas ļauns Eenaidneex nhe warr kaiteht / Kas to ghrib / 
tas ẜacka Amen.

XXVI.
@v{Vom Tod vnd Sterben.}
@v{HERR nun leſſeſtu deinen Diener.}
KVnx nu leetz tu tawu Kallpu meerige braukt / Ka tu ẜatziyis
eſẜi.

Kattru tu ẜattaiſẜiyis eſẜi wiſẜeems Ļaudeems.
Weenu ghaißmu apghaißmoht tohs Paggaņus / Vnd par ghodu
taweems Ļaudeems Jſra?l.

@v{HERR JEſu CHriſt wahr Menſch vnd GOtt.}
Vnx JEſu CHriſt Czillwähx vnd Deews / Katters tu czeeti
mohkas vnd Mehdiſchanu / Mannis dehļ py Kruſtu eſẜi nomirris
/ Vnd mann tawa Tähwa ſchälaſtibu nopellniyis.
2 . Es luhdſu czaur tawu Ruhktu mohku / Tu ghribbi mann
Ghrähzeneekam ſchehliex buht / Kad es nu nahku eekſchan mirrſchanu
bähdams / Vnd czienieſchohß ar to Nawu.
3. Kad mann nobahl wiß mans Waix / vnd mannas Auſẜis nhe
dſirrd wairs / Kad manna Mehle wairahk nhe runna / Vnd mann
no bailibu mannu Ꞩirrdi ẜalauſch.
4. Kad mans Prahtz wairs nhe attſinnahß / Vnd nhe weena
Czillwäka Palliex mann klaht ſtahw / Tad nahtz O Kunx CHriſte
mann dries / Par Palligu mannà paſtarà ghallà.
5. Vnd wedd mann aran ſcho behdigu dſiewoſchanu / Pa=ihſẜini
mann tahs Nahwes Wahrgoſchanu / Tohs ļaunus Gharrus no
mannim dſenn / Ar tawu Gharru allaſch py mann palleetz.

Kunx eekſchan tawu Rohku / dohd mannai Meeſẜi labbu duſẜeſchanu
/ Teekams ta paſtara Deena nahk turr klaht.
@b{7. Weenu}

[387.lpp.]
	7. Weenu preezigu Aukſchamczellſchanu mann dohd / Eekſchan
paſtaru Deenu mann aisbilldini / vnd mannus Ghräkus wairs nhe 
peemini / No ſchälaſtibas mann to muhſchigu dſiewoſchanu dohd.
	8. Ka tu mann eſẜi ſohliyis / Eekſchan tawu Wahrdu / to es töw
titzu / Patteeß / pattees es ẜacku jums / Kas mannu Wahrdu turr
vnd titz mann. 
	9. Tas nhe nahx eekſchan to Ꞩohdibu / Vnd to Nahwu muhſcham
nhe baudieß / vnd jeb tas ſcheitan laizige mirrſt / Tam nhe 
buhß tomähr tapehtz ißniekt.
	10. Bett es ghribbu ar ſtippru Rohku / To ißraut aran tahs
Nahwes ẜaites / Vnd py ẜöw jembtees ẜawà Wallſtibà / Turr buhß

	11. Eekſchan preezibu dſiewoht muhſchige : Turr palliedſi

Palliedſi ka mehs ghaidam no Ꞩirdtz.

aiſmickt czaur JEſum CHriſtum / Amen.
