@b{3. Ock}

[391.lpp.]
	3. Ock manns Kunx JEſu CHriſt / Katters tu tick rahme / 
Mannis dehļ py Kruſtu eſẜi nomirris / Vnd mann to Däbbäſẜu attpirzis
/ vnd mums wiſẜeems ween lieds / To muhſchigu ſchälaſtibu.
	4. Amen ick kattrà ſtundà / ẜacku es no Ꞩirrdtz dibben / Tu ghribbätu
mums waddiet / Kunx CHriſte allaſchien / Ka mehs tawu 
Wahrdu / Muhſchige warram ſlahweht / Amen.

@v{Jch weiß ein ewigs Himmelreich.}
		ES ſinnohß weenu muhſchigu Däbbäſſa=wallſtibu / Tha gir 
		iht krahßne darrita / Nhe no Ꞩuddrabu neds ẜarrkanu Sälltu
/ Ar Deewa Wahrdu muhräta.
	2. Eekſchan to dſiewo Deewa Dähls / Tas Behrnings JEſus
CHriſtus / Vs kattru wiſẜa manna czerriba gir / Kamehr es py
to nahku. 
	3. Es äßmu weens nabbax Czeļļa=wiers / Buhß ſtaighaht ẜawu
czeļļu / Eekſchan to muhſchigu Tähwa Semm / Es luhdſcho
mann nhe attſtaht.
	4. Ar mannu Aſẜini eſẜi tu attpeſtietz / Es myļo töw no Ꞩirdtz / 
Eſẜi paczeetiex tawohß bähdohß / Es ghribbu parwehrt tawas ẜahpes.

	5. Kad tu eſẜi Deewabiyatais / vnd ey py laiku / Py to ſwätu 
Deewaghalldu / Wiſẜus tawus Ghräkus vnd Noſegummus / Es 
nhe ghribbu wairs peeminneht.
	6. Jeb no töw wiſẜi Czillwäki / Attkahp ſcheit wirſẜon Semmes
/ Es ghribbu tow pa ẜahneem buht / Taws Preex vnd ghellbeſchana
tapt.
	7. Raudaſchana by manns pirrmais Ballxnis / Ar Raudaſchanu
es peedſimmu / Ar Raudaſchanu näß mann attkall nohſt / Teems 
Tahrpeems par Barribu.
	8. Tomähr es ſinnu ka ſchy manna Meeſẜa / Eekſchan Kappu 
nhe pallix / Paſtarà deenà no jaukeems Engeļeems / Vsmohdenata
py muhſchigu Preeku. 
	@b{9. Turr}

[392.lpp.]
	9. Turr palliedſi mums JEſus CHriſt / Katters muhſẜo dehļ 
eſẜi mirris / Vnd mums ar tawu ruhktu Nahwu / To Däbbäſẜo=
wallſtibu attpirzis.
	10. Laideeta mums wiſẜi lieds / Tam Kungam luhkt no Ꞩirdtz
dibben / Par ẜawu leelu lehnibu / czaur JEſum CHriſtum / Amen.

@v{Ach wie elend iſt vnſer Zeit.}
		OCk ka behdiga gir muhſẜo dſiewoſchana / Scheitan wirſẜon
		ſchahs Semmes :/: Ghann peepehſch tas Czillwähx peeghullahß
/ Mums buhs wiſẜeems nomirrth: Scheitan eekſchan
ſchahs Wahrgoſemmes / gir wiſẜur Bähdi vnde Darrbs / Jeb töw
ghann labb ißdohdahs.
	2. Ock Adama Krittums vnd Noſegummi / To wiſẜu vs mums
czehle :/: Ock Deews mahzi tu mums / Ka mehs to pareiſe attſieſtam:
Ka mehs tick ackli vnd ſtullbi äſẜam / patt Nhelaimes widdu buhdami
/ Nhe gir tas leels brienums ? 
	3. Kunx Deews tu muhſẜo ghellbeſchana eſẜi / Tawu Palligu 
mums ẜuhti :/: Aiſto tu tawus Ļaudis nhe aismirrſti / Kattri ẜöw
py töw ghreeſchahs: Ar tawu Gharru ſtahwi mums klaht / Weenu
ſchehligu Stundinyu arridſan dohd / czaur JEſum CHriſtum / 
Amen.
			
XXVII.
@v{Vom Begräbniß.}
@v{Mit Fried vnd Frewd ich fahr dahin.}
		AR Meeru vnd Preeku es brautſcho proyam / Eekſchan Deewa 
		Prahtu / Drohſcha gir manna Ꞩirrdtz vnd Prahtz / Weegla
		vnd kluſẜa / Ka Deews mann ẜohliyis gir / Ta Nahwe gir 
manns Meex tappis. 
@b{2. To}

[393.lpp.]
	2. To darra CHriſtus patteeſẜa Deewa Dähls / Tas yhſtäns
Peſtitais / Kattru tu mann / O Kunx / eſẜi litzis rädſäht / Vnd mahzi
paſiet / Ka tas äſẜohtz ta Dſiewiba vnd Peſtiſchana / Eekſchan bähdahms
vnd arridſan eekſchan mirrſchanu.
	3. To eſẜi tu wiſẜeems paradiyis / Ar leelu ſchälaſtibu / Py tawu 
Wallſtibu to wiſẜu paſẜaul / Litzis aitzeenaht / czaur tawu ſwähtu
dargu Wahrdu / Katters gir wiſẜahs mallahs attſkanneyis.
	4. Wings gir ta Peſtiſchana vnd ſwäta ghaißma / Preekſchan
teems Paggaņeems / Apghaißmoht tohs kattri töw nhe paſieſt / 
Vnd ghanniet / Wings gir tawo ļauſcho Jſraeļa / ſlawa / ghohtz / 
Preex vnd Liexmiba.

@v{Mitten wir im Leben ſind.}
		PAtt labbà dſiewoſchanà / Mums ta Nahwe ẜayämm :/: Kurr
		mehs meckleyam kas pallieds / ka mehs ſchalaſtibu attrohdam / 
		Tas eſẜi tu Kunx weens / Muhſẜe Noſeegummi gir mums
ſchähl / Kattri töw Kunx apkaitenayuſchi gir / Swähtz Kunx Deews / 
Swähtz warräns Deews / Swähtz ſchehligais Peſtitais / tu muhſchiex
Deews / Nhe leetz mums eeghrimbt / Eekſchan tahs ruhktas 
Nahwes bähdams / Kyrie eleiſon.
	2. Nahwes Widdu kahrdena / Mums tahs Elles Ryekle :/: Kas
ghribb mums no tahdeems bähdeems / Attkall atpeſtiet ? To darri tu
Kunx weens / ſchähl gir tawai ſchälaſtibai / Muſẜi Ghräki vnd leela
Waina: Swähtz Kunx Deews / Swähtz warräns Deews / Swähtz
ſchehligais Peſtitais / Tu muhſchiex Deews / Nhe laid mums iſẜamiſtees
/ Par to dſiļļu Elles Werrßmi / Kyrie eleiſon.
	3. Widdu eekſchan Elles bailibas / muhſẜi Ghräki mums eedſänn :/: 
Kurr buhs mums tad nobähkt / kurr mehs warram pallickt? Py töw
Kunx CHriſte ween / Tawu dahrgu Aſẜini eſẜi tu ißlehyis / Katters
par wiſẜu Ghräku ghann darra / Swähtz Kunx Deews / Swähtz
warräns Deews / Swähtz ſchehligais Peſtitais / tu muhſchiex Deews
Nhe laid mums no alloteeß / No to ihſtanu Titzibu / Kyrie eleiſon.

[394.lpp.]
@v{Nun laſtvns den Leib begraben.}
		NV laideeta mums to Mirroni aprackt / Par to nhe kahdu Jſẜamiſẜeſchanu
turreht / Tas Jaunà=deenà attkal aukſcham
czellſẜeeß / vnd nhe ẜatruhdähtz preekſchan nahx.
	2. Semme gir tas / vnd no tahs Semmes / Par Semm tas attkal
taps / Vnd no tahs Semmes attkal aukſcham czellẜeeß / Kad
Deewa Baſune attſkannehs.
	3. Wiņja Dwehſẜele dſiewo muhſchiege eekſchan Deewu / katters
to ſcheit aran tyhras ſchälaſtibas / No wiſẜeems Ghräkeems vnd Noſeegummeems
/ czaur ẜawu Dählu attpeſtiyis gir.
	4. Wiņja Bähdi / Nhelaimiba vnd Waidi / Gir dabbuyuſchi
ẜawu labbu ghallu / Wings gir neſẜis Chriſti Naßtu / Gir nomirris
vnd dſiewo wehl. 
	5. Ta Dwehſẜele dſiewo beß wiſẜas ſuhdſeſchanas / Ta Meeſẜa
ghull ihs tai Jaunai=deeni / Kad Deews to apſkaidrohß / Vnd
muhſchigu Preeku tay dohß.
	6. Scheit gir tas Czillwäx bähdohß biyis / Bett turr tas attkall
attſpirx / Eekſchan muhſchigu Preeku vnd Liexmibu / Spiedehs 
ka ta ſpohſcha Ꞩaule.
	7. Nun attſtayam mehs to ſcheit ghulloht / Vnd eetham mahyahs
ẜawu czeļļu / ẜattaiſẜameeß arridſan ar wiſẜu Ꞩirdi / Aiſto ta 
Nahwe mums arridſan pee=eedt.
	8. To pallieds mums CHriſtus muſẜo Preex / Katters mums 
czaur ẜawu Aſẜini gir attpeſtiyis / No tha Wälla Spähku vnd muhſchigu
Mohku / Tam gir Ꞩlawa / Ghohtz vnd Patteitziba allaſchien
/ Amen.

@v{So laſt vns den Leib behalten.}
TAd laideeta mums to Meeſẜu abghlabboht / Deews wiņja
Dwehſẜel ẜarrgahß / Tas ween to apghahdahß / Ka wings to
ſinna / bett mehs nhe prohtam.
@b{2. To}

[395.lpp.]
	2. To czerreyam mehs vnd titzam / Ka mehs wehl attkall redſeſẜimeeß
/ Kad mehs czellſẜimees no tahs Semmes / vnd preekſchan
Ꞩhodu nahxim.
	3. Nu ghulli / teekams Deews töw vnd wiſẜeems / Ꞩawu Baſun
lix dſirrdeht / Ka wiſẜo preekſcha taps laſẜietz / Kas ſläppäne gir 
notitzis. 
	4. Deews palliedſi mums ka mehs wiſẜi lieds / Eekſchan Titzibas
dſiewoyam ghohdige / Pehtz preezige no ſchennenes ſkirram / Vnd 
preekſchan tawu Ꞩohdibu labbe paſtahweyam / Amen.

@v{Ein anders.}
O JEſu wiſẜas Paſẜaules Eeẜakums / Nu eepreezini mums
kattri mehs noſkummuſſchi äſẜam / Czaur tawu ruhktu
Nahwu / Vnd palliedſi mums Kunx no wiſẜahms bähdams / 
Ka mehs nhe ẜamaitayam / Kad mums buhß nomirrth / Kyrie
eleiſon.

@v{Collecta beym Grabe.}
O Wiſẜewallditais Kunx vnd Deews / Katters tu
mums czaur to Mutt tawa ſwähta Apustuļa Pawila
eſẜi mahziyis / ka mums par teems kattri eekſchan
CHriſto duß / nhe buhs bähdateeß : Mehs luhdſam
thöw / ka mehs ar wiſẜeems Titzigeems warram weßti
tapt eekſchan to muhſchigu Preeku / Kad taws Dähls
nahx Ꞩohdiet tohs dſiewus vnd Mirronus / czaur ta paſſcha
tawa myļa Dähla muhſẜa Kungha JEſu CHriſti
ruhktu Mohkams vnd Nawu / Amen.

@v{Ein anders.}
O Wiſſewallditais Kunx vnd Deews / Katters tu
czaur to nomirrſchanu tawa Dähla tohs Ghrä@b{kus}


[396.lpp.]
kus vnd to Nahwu par ſmeeklu darriyis / vnd czaur wiņja
Aukſchamczellſchanu to Nhenoſeedſibu vnd to muhſchigu
dſiewoſchanu attkal attneſẜis eſẜi / ka mehs no tha
Wälla Spähku attpeſtiti / vnd czaur to paſſchu Aukſcham
czellſchanu irr muhſẜai Meeſẜi no teems mirroņeems
attkal buhs vsmohdenatai tapt : Dohd mums
ſchehlige / Ka mehs to ſtippre vnd no wiſẜas Ꞩirdtz titzam
/ vnd to preezigu Aukſchamczellſchanu muhſẜas
Meeſẜas ar wiſẜeems ſwähteems dabbuith warram / 
czaur to paſſchu tawu myļu Dählu muhſẜu Kunghu
JEſum CHriſtum / Amen. 

XXVIII.
@v{Vom Jüngſten Tage vnd ewigen}
@v{Leben.}
@v{Wacht auff ihr Chriſten alle / Wacht auff.}
VSmohſteeta wiſẜi juhß Chriſtiti Ļaudis / Vsmohſteeta no
wiſẜas Ꞩirdtz :/: Eekſchan ſchahs Wahrgoſemmes / Vsmohſteeta
/ nu gir leels laix : Tas Kunx dries nahx / Ta deena meckle
ẜawu Wackaru / Tohs Ghräzeneekus tas paſuddenahß / Kas
warr preekſchan to paſtahweht.
	2. Nauda / Mannta nhe darries labb / Mums nhe palliedſehß
muhſẜa Leppniba :/: Töw buhs to dries attſtaht / Kad nahk ta ruhkta
Nahwe : Jeb gir töw ghann jaux Waix / Jeb eſẜi tu jauns vnd 
baggahtz / Deews warr töw peepehſche ẜamaitaht / Eekſchan weenu
Atzis mircklu.
@b{3. Tapehtz}

[397.lpp.]
3. Tapehtz wiſẜi juhß Chriſtiti Ļaudis / Kattri juhß ſcheitan kohpa
eſẜeta :/: Attſtayeeta no juhſẜu Leppnibu / Vnd ghaideeta vs juhſẜu
laiku : Ghribbaht juhß py Deewu dſiewoht / Tad meckleyeeta to
muhſchigu baggatibu / Wings jums to baggatige dohs / Vnd palliedſehß
no wiſẜahms bähdahms. 
	4. Deewa Wahrdtz gir mums dohtz / Aran tyhras ſchälaſtibas
:/: Ka mums pehtz to buhß dſiewoht / Vnd ẜöw ẜattaiſẜiteeß:
Tad laideeta mums to wära jembt / Vnd ar to Ꞩirrdi py
to peelipt / Ja mehs no to attkahpſim / Tad äſẜam mehs paſuſti.

	5. Ock nhe buhtu tas peedſimmis / Katters Deewa Wahrdu
pullgo :/: Tas gir wiſkim ſamaitahtz / Vnd ſtaigha patt nacktz widdu
: Pills Ghräko vnd Kauno / Vnd apſmey to Deewa Wahrdu / 
O way tay leelai Nhelaimibai / Wiņja Dweſẜele palleek muhſchige
paſuſta.
	6. Tohs Nabbagus kattri py jums dſiewo / Tohß vsluhkoyeeta
:/: Tee jums leelu Kaunu darries / Kad juhß Ꞩohda ſtahwehſẜeeta
: To buhs jums arridẜan ſinnaht / Ka Deews nhe gir no maxatins
/ Vnd kas teems Nabbageems gir labbe darriyis / Tas turr ẜawu
Allgu dabbuis.

@v{iſt gewißlich an der Zeit.}
PAttees nu buhß tas ihſtäns laix / Ka Deewa Dähls atteeß :/: 
Eekſchan ẜawas leelas Ghodibas / Ꞩohdiet tohß labbus vnd 
ļaunus: Tad nhe buhs ſmeeſchanas laix / Kad wiſẜas leetas 
ar Vgauni ẜaddex / Ka Peteris no to raxta.
	2. Baſunes dſirrdehs attſkannam / Pa wiſẜas Paſẜaules ghallam
:/: Tad tudeļļ aukſcham czellſẜeeß / Wiſẜi Mirroņi peepehſch: 
Bett tee kattri wehl dſiewi gir / Tohs tas Kunx weenà Atzes mirckly / 
Parwehrtieß vnd attiaunahß.
	3. Pehtz to weenu ghramatu nolaſẜies / Eekſchan kattru gir 
eeraxtietz :/: Ko wiſẜi Czillwäki jauni vnd Wätzi / Wirſẜon Semmes
@b{gir} 

[398.lpp.]
gir darriyuſchi: Tad ick kattris patteeſẜe / Dſirrdehs ko tas gir ſtradayis
/ Kamähr tas ſcheit gir dſiewoyis.
4. O Way tam paſſcham katters gir / Ta Kungha Wahrdu
nitzinayis :/: Vnd ween wirſẜon Semmes rietohs vnd wackarohß / 
Vs leelu Manntu domayis : Tas pattees itt plix pallix / Vnd buhs 
ar to Wällu eedt / No CHriſto eekſchan Elles.
	5. O JEſu palliedſi tanny laikà / Pehtz tawu ruhktu Mohku :/: 
Ka es eekſchan ſchälaſtibas ghramatus / Eeraxtietz tohpu attraſts: 
To es arridſan ſtippre titzu / Aiſto tu eſẜi to Wällu ẜohdiyis / Vnd 
mannu Parradu nomaxayis.
	6. Tapehtz eſẜi tu manns Aisbilldetais / Kad tu nu attkall atteeſẜi
:/: Vnd laſẜi mann no tahs Ghramatas / Eekſchan kattras 
tawi Titzigi raxtiti gir : Ka es ar ẜaweems Brahliſcheems / Eekſchan
tawu Däbbäſẜu warru ee=eedt / Kattru tu mums eſẜi nopellniyis.

	7. Kad es / O Kunx / ẜawus Ghräkus apdohmayu / Mannas
Atztinyas Aſẜarus rittina :/: Bett kad es to muhſchigu Preeku apdohmayu
/ Manna Ꞩirdtz liexmodameeß vslätz: Palliedſi Kunx / ka
es tawu Waigu / Warru redſeht ar ẜaweems Atzeems / Eekſchan to 
muhſchigu dſiewoſchanu.
	8. O JEſu CHriſt tu illge kahwe / Ar tawu Paſtaru=deenu :/: 
Teems Czillwäkeems tohp ļohte bail / No leelu Waidu vs Semmes:
Nahtz tock / nahtz tock tu leels Ꞩohgis / Vnd attpeſty mums 
ſchehlige / No wiſẜu ļaunu / Amen. 

XXIX
@v{Morgends Geſänge.}
@v{Jch danck dir lieber HERE / daß du.}
ES patteitſchu töw myļais Kunx / Ka tu mann eſẜi paſẜarghayis
:/: Tahda breeßmigà Nackty / Mann tick czeete ghulloht:
@b{Ar}

[399.lpp.]
Ar Tumſẜibu parjämbtz / Ta lieds leelà lixtà / No kattras es ißbehdſis
äßmu / Tu Kunx vnd Deews mann palliedſeyi.
	2. Es töw ghribbu patteickt vnd ſlahweht / O tu mans Deews 
vnd Kunx :/: Eekſchan auxtu Däbbäſẜu / Vnd töw no Ꞩirdtz luhdſcho
/ Scho deen mann arridſan paſẜarrgi / Pehtz tawu ſchehligu 
Prahtu / Waddi mann tawà czeļļà / Vnd lohki mannu dabbu.
	3. Ka es Kunx nhe noghreeſchohs / No tawu yhſtänu czeļļu :/: 
Tas Wälls mann nhe parghluna / Mann malldiet wäſdams: Vsturri
mann czaur tawu Lehnibu / To es töw no Ꞩirdtz luhdſcho / 
Par Wälla Willtibu vnd blehdibu / Ar kattru tas prett man ſtahw.
	4. To Titzibu mann arridſan dohd / Vs tawu Dählu JEſum 
CHriſtum :/: Mannus Ghräkus mann arridſan peedohd / Scheitan 
taggadien : To tu mann nhe aisleexi / Ka tu mann ẜohliyis eſẜi / Tam 
by mannus Ghräkus nohſt jembt / Vnd peſtiet no to Naßtu.
	5. To czerribu mann arridſan dohd / Kattra nhe leek ẜamaitaht
:/: Ta lieds to Chriſtitu myläſtibu / Prettieb to kas mann ļaun 
darra : Ka es tam attkall labbe darru / Nhe mäcklädams mannu 
Auglu / Vnd myļoyo to ka ẜöw paſſchu / Ka tas töw pa prahtam 
gir. 
	6. Leetz mann tawu Wahrdu paſluddenaht / Schynny beßdeewigà
Paſẜauleh :/: Vnd mann tawu Kallpu dehweht / Nhe byhtees 
kahdu Warru neds Naudu: Kattra man dries warrätu no ghreeſt / 
No tawas tyhras Taißnibas / Tu mann arridſan nhe noſkirr / No 
tahs Chriſtitas Draudſibas.
	7. Laid mann to Deenu pabeickt / Tawam Wahrdam par ſlawu
:/: Ka es no töw nhe noſkirros / Lieds ghallam py töw palleeku: 
Paſẜargi mannu Meeſẜu vnd Dwehſẜel / Vnd to Labbibu vs lauku / 
Ko tu mann eſẜi dewiß / Tas gir wiß tawà Rohkà.
	8. Kunx CHriſt ghodu es töw ẜacku / Par wiſẜu tawu labbe darriſchanu
:/: Ko tu mann wiſẜu mannu muhſchu / Wiſẜahdà weetà 
paradiyis eſẜi : Tawu Wahrdu es ghribbu ghodaht / Tu weens eſẜi 
labbs / Ar Tawu Meeſẜu mann ähdini / Ar tawu Aſẜini mann dſirrdini.
@b{9. Töw}

[400.lpp.]
9. Töw ween peedärr tas Ghohtz / Töw ween peedärr ta Teickſchana
:/: Ta Attreepſchana töw palleek / Tu weens mums ſwehti: 
Kad mehs meerige apghullam / Ar ſchälaſtibu py mums ſteidſeeß / 
Dohd mums ar Titzibu prettie ſtahweht / Kad mums tas Wälls 
vseedt. 

@v{Jch danck dir ſchon durch deinen.}
ES patteitſchu töw krahßne / czaur tawu Dählu / O Deews 
par tawu Lehnibu / Ka tu mann eſẜi ſchinny Nackty / Tick 
ſchehlige paſẜargayis.
	2. Kad es ghulleyu tick czeete / Ar Tumbſẜibu apjämbtz / No 
wiſẜeems Ghräkeems mohzietz tappu / Kattrus es ẜawu muhſchu äßmu
darriyis.
3. Tapehtz es luhdſchu no Ꞩirdß dibben / Tu ghribbätu mann 
peedohd / Wiſẜus mannus Ghräkus kattrus es äßmu darriyis / Ar 
ẜawu nicknu dſiewoſchanu. 
	4. Vnd gribbätu arridſan ſcho deen / Mann ghellbeht vnd

@v{Gemeine Collecte:}
O Wiſẜewalldiex Deews / muhſchiex Tähws /

tees Deews allaſchien vnd muhſchige / Amen.

@b{Eſẜi}

[419.lpp.]
Eſẜi mums ſchehliex Deews / eſẜi mums ſchehliex: 
Aiſto vs töw pallaiſchahß ẜöw muhſẜa Dweſẜele / vnd appackſchan
to ähnu tawo Spahrno gir mums Paglabhpſchana
/ teekams ta Nhelaime pahreet.
Steidſees Deews mums peſtiet / Kunx nahtz nahkdams
mums palliedſeht.
Kunx katters tu czittu reis arridſan eſẜi wiſẜu tawu 
Dußmibu nohſt mettis / vnd ẜöw ghreeſees no to bahrſẜibu
ẜawas Dußmibas / Eepreezini mums / Deews 
muhſẜo Peſtitais / vnd attlaidees no tawas Nheſchälaſtibas
par mums.
Kunx parrahdi mums tawu ſchälaſtibu / vnd palliedſi
mums. 
Attpeſti mums muhſẜas Ꞩeewas / muhſẜus Bährnus
vnd Ꞩaim / muhſẜus{wuhſẜus} Kaimiņņus vnd Draugus / no 
wiſẜu ļaunu / vnd to nicknu Ꞩährgu vnd Nheweſẜelibu. 
Nhe leetz mums ißbietees par teems Schauſſchaleems
kattri nackties pahreet / par tahms bulltahms / kattri
Deenà ſkraida / par to Ꞩährgu kattra Deenas widdu 
ẜamaita.
Nhe leetz mums kadu ļaun notickt / neds kahdai 
Ꞩährgai py muhſẜams buhdams peeſtahtees. Pawehl 
tawam Engeļam / ka tas mums paſẜarrga vs wiſẜu muhſẜu
czeļļu.
Pilldini mums ſchehlige ar Weſẜelibu / vnd rahdi 
mums tawu Peſtiſchanu.
@b{Par}

[420.lpp.]
Par nicknu peepehſchu Nahw paſẜarrgi mums mieļais
Deews vnd Kunx.
Eeſiemo ar tawu Ꞩirrdtzmieliga Dähla muhſẜa 
Kungha JEſu Chriſti Aſẜini muhſẜas Ꞩirrdes / ka tas 
Mehrdehtais Engels mums czätzen eet.
Eeſiemo muhſẜas Dwehſẜeles ar to Spähku ẜawa 
wißſwähta Kruſta / vnd Nahw / ka mums nhekada Nhelaimiba
nhenoteek.
Czaur tawa Dähla Kruſtu vnd Nahwu / palliedſi 
mums mieļais Kunx vnd Deews. 
Ꞩacki vs to Ꞩamaitatayu / jaw ghann gir / Attrau 
ẜawu Rohku.
Bett ja mums tad pehtz tawu labbu prahtu no 
ſchennenes eet buhß / vnd py muhſẜeems Tähweems ẜackrahteems
tapt / Tad laid tas palleek muhſẜo pehdeis 
Wahrtz / ka mehs ẜackam : Eekſchan tawu Rohku pawehļam
mehs muhſẜu Dwehſẜel / Tu eſẜi mums attpeſtiyis / 
Kunx tu peetitziegs Deews.
Packlauſẜi mums mieļais Kunx vnd Deews / aiſto 
tu eſẜi jo muhſẜo Tähws.
Abſchäloyees töw par mums / aiſto tu eſẜi jo muhſẜo 
Eepreezetais vnd Palliex eekſchan bähdahms.
Paſẜarrgi mums / aiſto tu eſẜi jo weens Wißſpähziex

@v{Das 12. Capittel des Propheten Eſaiae.}
@v{Jch dancke dir HErr / das du zornig biſt geweſen vber} @l{etc.}
ES patteitzo töw Kunx / ka tu Dußmiex eſẜi vs mann biyis / 
vnd tawa Dußmiba attghreeſuſẜees gir / vnd eepreezini mann. 
		2. Redſi / Deews gir mans Peſtitais / es äßmu ar meeru / 
vnd nhe bieſtohs / Aiſto Deews tas Kunx gir manns Spähx / vnd 
manna Dſeeßma / vnd gir manns Peſtitais.
	3. Juhß eeẜeeta preezadammees Vhdeni ſmellt / no teems Awoteems
tahs Peſtiſchanas.
	4. Vnd ẜatzieſẜeeta tanny laikà / Patteitzeeta tam Kungam / ißẜautzeeta
winja Wahrdu / Darrait ſinnamu ſtarrpan teems Ļaudeems
winja Darrbu / paſluddenayeeta ka winja Wahrtz tick auxtz gir. 
	5. Dſeedaita tam Kungam / aiſto Wings gir ẜöw kraßne paradiyees
/ to buhs ſinnaht wiſẜahm Semmehm.
@b{6. Liex-}

[432.lpp.]
	6. Liexmo vnd teitz tu Dſiewotaya eekſchann Zion / Aiſto tas 
ſwähtz Jſraël gir leels py töw.
Ghohtz gir tam Tähwam / vnd tam Dählam / vnd tam ſwähtam
Gharram / ka no Eeẜakumu gir biyis / vnd palleek muhſcho 
muhſcham / Amen.
	
@l{FINIS.}
@l{Summa DEo Soli gloria, laus}
@l{& honor.}
